Clap! The finger light's force left thunder-like sounds.

The power of the finger light could be considered extremely strong in Stage Seventeen. It was also at the top in Stage Twenty-eight, but it was no longer as terrifying as it was in Stage Seventeen.

However, the Primeval Lord of Heaven had experienced many battles. His experience harnessed not only his instincts, but also his skills. The finger light that pierced through the armor of the Moon Fire Slaves accurately pierced into the flames and through their spiritual cores.

"Crack, crack, crack..."

The nine Moon Fire Slaves that surrounded them from all directions froze in place.

After a few seconds, the flames that were emitted from the armor gradually shrank, disappeared, and extinguished.

The Moon Fire Slaves were a kind of fire spirits, and the flames were their forms. Since their spiritual cores were broken and their flame bodies disappeared, the powerful armor on their bodies collapsed and fell to the ground.

The Soul of Light and the several Twilight Mice that had deceived Zen into coming in were all stunned. Their eyes were in a sort of daze and confusion was evident on their faces.

What had just happened was indeed unexpected, for they really looked up to the Moon Fire Slaves. In fact, in their eyes, the Moon Fire Slaves were invincible.

No one in Stage Twenty-eight could resist them. Even the ruler of Stage Twenty-eight couldn't resist the joint attack of several Moon Fire Slaves.

It should have been a piece of cake for the nine Moon Fire Slaves to kill two human beings, who had mere physical bodies, in a confined space.

But in a flash, the nine Moon Fire Slaves were killed! Their shock was unmatched. Amongst the crowd were gasps, dropped jaws, and pale faces.

"Kill them! Kill them!" the Soul of Light ordered desperately, once he realized what had just happened.

He had a high status, but after all, he was just a Soul of Light. It was impossible for him to fight against Elvinia and Zen.

Following the man's order, those Twilight Mice all determinedly rushed towards Zen and Elvinia.

Zen's eyes narrowed slightly. He lowered his body and jumped high towards the sky. His feet landed directly on the top of the head of the Twilight Mouse positioned in front.

Boom! The Twilight Mouse's head was directly crushed.

Zen didn't stop. With a crisp crack of lightning, his fist had already smashed into the head of another Twilight Mouse.

Boom! Boom! Boom! His body flashed a few times, and the several Twilight Mice had lost their heads.

The Soul of Light's eyes widened as he watched the Twilight Mice being killed one by one by Zen. Then, he realized that he should withdraw from the Other Shore.

Just as he began to recite the Illusion Breaking Rune, he saw a handful of green sand pouring over like rain. The Soul Restraining Sand fell on the surface of his Soul of Light, locking him on the Other Shore. Now, as much as he wanted to leave, he couldn't.

Elvinia clapped her hands to clean up the Soul Restraining Sand between her fingers. A small smile curled on her lips as she asked, "All this makes me want to know who will die now, us or you?"

The Soul of Light's desire to survive was very strong. After realizing that he was unable to leave the Other Shore, he turned around and wildly ran towards a passageway in the cave.

After all, he had been trained in the Soul City, so his escape speed was not slow.

If he met another person, he might have been able to escape, but unfortunately, he met Zen.

Crack! Accompanied by a loud bolt of lightning, Zen suddenly appeared beside him. He stretched out his hand and gently pulled the Soul of Light. He was like a kite with a broken string, weightless, and was easily thrown back by Zen.

"Let, let me go..." the man pleaded. His heart was pounding tremendously against his chest, and he struggled to catch his breath.

"Besides ambushing us here, does the Element Spirit race have any other plans?" Zen asked in a firm tone. His eyes were sharp, as if they were to pierce through whatever lies this man might stutter.

"No, no!" the man answered immediately, afraid that Zen didn't believe him. Fear was reflected in his eyes. Zen tried to look deeper to see if there was malice in his answer. He then added, "Who would have thought that so many Moon Fire Slaves couldn't do anything to you? I thought even one Moon Fire Slave would be enough. What had happened was beyond my imagination."

"Is this really the northwest corner of the Forbidden Rain City?" Zen asked again. He was still unsure whether to trust this man's answers, but he needed to understand the situation better.

"Yes. You will reach it as long as you go up through this passage. There are some Twilight Mice along the way but with your strength, you can pass through smoothly," the man said.

Zen glanced at Elvinia, whose eyes flashed with killing intent. Elvinia nodded at him and a small smile formed on her thin and sharp lips.

Before the man could react, Zen's arms slightly curled his head.

Pop! The Soul of Light was like a fragile bubble, shattering and disappearing in the blink of an eye.

They didn't really care who this person was. Since he was a human, it was most likely that he came from the Bearing race or the Divine Farmer race.

As for where the real Doyle was and whether he was killed or not, they could only investigate after they left the Other Shore.

Following the direction given by the Soul of Light, Zen and Elvinia soon saw flat steps. Their every move was done with caution and all their senses were alert. After climbing up a certain distance, they heard some squeaks ahead. Then, bean-sized eyes floated from the darkness on both sides of the steps.

Sure enough, as the man said, there scattered many Twilight Mice in this passageway.

"Those Moon Fire Slaves are all dead below. I wouldn't mind killing the entire Twilight Mouse race as well. If you don't want to die, you can come up," Zen said coldly. His eyes were sharp and alert and he said those words in all seriousness.

Squeak! Squeak! Squeak! The Moon Fire Slaves were arranged by the Twilight Mice. The Twilight Mice were shocked when they heard that all nine of the Moon Fire Slaves had been killed.

Even as creatures of Stage Twenty-eight on the Other Shore, they were still not qualified to participate in a battle of this level. Moreover, the Element Spirit race did not give an order to let them attack Zen and Elvinia.

Squeaks echoed and soon, the eyes glowing in the darkness disappeared one by one.

After the Twilight Mice left, Zen continued to walk up with Elvinia. After they came out from a square well, they saw neatly arranged star rings.

"The Soul of Light didn't lie to us," Zen said, nodding his head slightly as he sized up the star rings.

In the Lust World, there were many star rings on each stage. Almost every ruling civilization had a star ring.

However, many civilizations were still not able to reach a high stage. Now that it was Stage Twenty-eight, the number of star rings had decreased significantly. There were only more than 100 star rings in front of them, which meant that only more than 100 ruling civilizations had once come here.

After finding the human race's star ring, Zen immediately threw himself into it. Elvinia immediately followed, imitating Zen's posture. Then, the two of them turned into two white lights and flew into the sky.

Stage Twenty-eight was under the rule of the Element Spirit race. If they knew that the Moon Fire Slaves had been killed, they would probably turn to the stage ruler. If that happened, there might be another fierce battle.

Thus, the earlier they left, the better.

In what seemed to be an instant, two beams of straight white light shuttled all the way and finally arrived at Stage Twenty-nine, where the Soul City was located.

Chapter 3711 The Boiling Blood A peak in blood-red color stood towering into the cloud. This was where the star ring of the human race was located.

The circle of light in the middle of the star ring quivered, and two figures suddenly appeared in its vicinity.

Once Zen's eyes adapted to the environment, he looked around and was instantly stunned.

On that peak, there was a circular platform with about seven or eight star rings at its center. The ones ascending to this place weren't limited to the human race; other races also ascended to this place. Dozens of Souls of Light crowded around the circular platform.

These Souls of Light had different forms. They belonged to various races, but for some reason, none of them belonged to the human race.

When they saw Zen's and Elvinia's corporeal bodies, their eyes lit up.

"These two people... They have corporeal bodies?"

"How do they do that?"

"That human girl seems to be an Other Shore creature?"

Since they could see Elvinia's features clearly, they naturally took her as an Other Shore creature.

Ignoring these Souls of Light, Zen walked to the edge of the round platform and looked around.

There were many blood-red peaks in the Constant Glory Stage. They were quite far away from each other and were surrounded by abysses. A lava-like red liquid flowed at the depth of those abysses.

"From Stage Twenty-nine to above, the Other Shore will be extremely dangerous," Elvinia, who stood beside him, spoke. "As you can see, the bottom of the Constant Glory Stage is filled with red liquid known as 'boiling blood', Any creature that comes into contact with it will completely melt away."

"But it isn't dangerous, is it?" Zen's gaze had already shifted from the bottom to the side of the peak. Paths that looked endless had been built among these peaks. As long as they didn't seek death and jump into the boiling blood, they would naturally be able to pass through safely.

Moreover, Zen could fly in the air, so it was naturally easier for him to pass through.

"Human friend, the boiling blood at the bottom isn't a big deal, but don't forget that there are still those Garudas in the sky!" A Soul of Light almost thirty feet tall suddenly came towards them.

"Garudas..."

Zen looked up.

Vaguely, shadows of giant birds could be seen flying about behind the clouds. However. Those birds seemed to do nothing else except circling around high in the sky.

"According to the information I've checked, we indeed have to be wary of them," Elvinia said as she nodded. "The Garudas are the most powerful creatures on the Constant Glory Stage. Even the Other Shore creatures are prey for those birds, let alone the Souls of Light."

Souls of Light were much more fragile than corporeal bodies. Even if one had entered Soul City, they would still be powerless—that was unless they could completely pass the test of Soul City, become a Colorless Soul, and enter the Holy Soul Realm.

"Yes, yes, yes! That's correct."

The thirty feet tall Soul of Light came over and said, "The situation on the Constant Glory Stage is too dangerous. We've been staying here waiting for a chance to go to the Soul City. Since you two have corporeal bodies, could you please escort us there?"

"I'm from the Wild Lion race. As long as you two are willing to escort me through, you just need to name your price..."

"……"

A hint of curiosity appeared on Zen's expression when he heard this. "Are you trapped here?"

"Yes! Those Garudas are cunning. We're safe only when we stay on this round platform. Once we step onto those paths, we'll be targeted by them,"

the member of the Wild Lion race said with a nod.

A smaller Soul of Light beside him had already come to the edge of the round platform. He quietly took a step towards the path and said, "See for yourself if you don't believe us!"

The Soul of Light had just stood on the path for a short while when a gust of wind swept down from above. A huge winged shadow rushed down at an incredible speed and then landed next to the path.

Nevertheless, the short Soul of Light managed to take back his foot before the Garuda rushed down.

"Chirp!"

The Garuda let out an angry cry. It then directed its beak fiercely towards the short Soul of Light to peck him.

However, the moment its beak crossed the edge of the platform, a streak of blood-red lightning emerged out of thin air along with sizzle noises. The Garuda let out a miserable cry, quickly flapped its wings, and rushed back to the sky, leaving behind a lingering burnt smell in the air.

"That's how it is," the short Soul of Light said.

The thirty-foot tall Soul of Light chuckled and said, "Jairo, the Garuda will certainly bear a grudge after you teased it like this. When you walk through the path, you'll be its first target."

Jairo said nonchalantly, "These birds are guarding this place all the time anyway. At worst, I'll just have to stay here for the rest of my life."

When Zen heard their conversation, it finally dawned on him that these people had probably been trapped here for quite a long time.

If the Constant Glory Stage had always been like this, it was theoretically impossible for them to get through.

He pondered the matter for a while and then said, "No, this is strange. If those Garudas have always been here, how did the others go to Soul City before?"

"Everyone can only wait for an opportunity," Elvinia said. "I heard that as long as there is blood fog, the Garudas will never want to come down. That being the case, when the blood fog spreads, everyone will quickly rush to the Soul City where they'll thus be safe!"

"Then how often does the blood fog occur?" Zen asked.

"We've stayed here for a long time, but we've yet to see the blood fog,"

another Soul of Light replied.

The appearance of the blood fog was completely random. Sometimes, the blood fog could spread for more than half of the Constant Glory Stage.

Sometimes, even though there was blood fog, it could only cover a portion of the area, so they still couldn't go to the Soul City.

"Then do you want us to fight against those strange birds?" Zen asked.

"Exactly!" the short Soul of Light said.

"It's too dangerous," Elvinia vetoed the idea. "Those Garudas are the most powerful creatures here. If they swarm over, you won't be able to defend yourself against them!"

Although she was confident in Zen, she didn't want him to take risks.

Elvinia's objection made those Souls of Light disappointed. One after another, they went back to their original positions. Some of them even chanted the Illusion Breaking Rune and withdrew from the Other Shore.

Right at this moment, the voice of the Primeval Lord of Heaven suddenly rang in Zen's mind. "This is really strange. Has the Blood Fog Spell already gone extinct in the Constant Glory Stage?"

"Blood Fog Spell? What is that?" Zen asked.

"Well, it seems that the Element Spirit race have worked hard over the years to erase a lot of things," the Primeval Lord of Heaven said with a helpless smile. "The Garudas on the Constant Glory Stage are indeed powerful.

Even the ruler of this stage is a Garuda. This is indeed a rare occurrence."

Generally speaking, the creatures in the Dark Region were much more powerful than the creatures in the Light Region. However, it was indeed rare that both the Dark Region and the Light Region of the Constant Glory Stage were dominated by Garudas.

Fortunately, the Garudas were very arrogant.

No matter how hard the Element Spirit race tried, they had never been able to win them over. Although these birds were dangerous and cruel, they didn't listen to the Element Spirit race.

The Garudas that stood on the top of the Constant Glory Stage were most afraid of the boiling blood in the abyss. In fact, most of the Other Shore creatures on the Constant Glory Stage relied on the boiling blood to survive.

After the Primeval Lord of Heaven told Zen the origins of the gigantic Garudas, he continued, "Long ago, someone had discovered that the blood fog could drive the Garudas away. Using the Blood Fog Spell to summon the boiling blood fog was practically the necessary means to pass through the Constant Glory Stage. I never expected that no one knows about it now."

Chapter 3712 Before The Gate The Other Shore hadn't always been the same. Since the Primeval Lord of Heaven and the others hadn't returned to the high stages in a long time, they didn't know that they had undergone earth-shattering changes.

Zen was hesitant now. He wondered whether he should listen to Elvinia and leave when the blood fog appeared, or just barge through.

It would be great if the Blood Fog Spell that the Primeval Lord of Heaven had mentioned really existed.

"Primeval Lord of Heaven, does the Blood Fog Spell still have an effect?"

Zen asked doubtfully.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven said, "You'll know when you try."

The Blood Fog Spell was similar to the Illusion Breaking Rune and was easy to master. Zen had mastered it in less than five minutes. He then walked to the edge of the round platform.

Elvinia and the others were confused at Zen's behavior and thought that he was about to tease the Garuda like the short Soul of Light.

But they heard Zen vaguely chant something.

While Zen had recited, the blood in the abyss at the foot of the mountain boiled even more fiercely, as if a fierce beast was emerging from it.

A trace of bright red blood floated up into the air.

Elvinia and the others gasped, their eyes widening in shock.

"How has the blood fog appeared so soon?"

"He can summon the blood fog?!"

"I've never heard of such a method before!"

The Blood Fog Spell was not a complicated method, but the Element Spirit race had erased it from history for a long time. There still remained a small number of people who had mastered this method, but no outsider knew of it.

As they watched the blood fog spreading, the Souls of Light rushed cheerily into the path.

But the blood fog seemed to consider Zen as the center and spread around him. It wouldn't move if Zen didn't move forward. This caused the Souls of Light to come to halt and wait for Zen to take the lead.

"Let's go," Zen said with a smile.

Elvinia, who was standing behind Zen, whispered to him, "Did that senior master teach you this?"

"Yeah," Zen said, nodding.

After he had carried the book, he had owned a number of abilities within himself that he couldn't explain. Elvinia knew the truth, and Zen also hadn't the slightest intention of hiding it from her.

They had no idea who had built the paths that connected those otherwise isolated peaks.

When the Garudas saw people moving ahead on the path below, they spread their wings and pounced down upon the path. But the moment they approached the blood fog, they flapped their wings and flew backwards, crying out in disgust.

As Zen and his companions moved along the path, the blood fog moved along with them.

It faded away about an hour after it started following Zen. At this, Zen chanted the Blood Fog Spell again, and the blood fog became denser and denser once again.

They had just passed the last peak when a huge blood-red peak loomed ahead of them. The surrounding small peaks were nothing compared to this one.

At the top of this peak was a huge platform, on which floated a blurry city.

"Is that the Soul City?" Zen muttered, looking at the blurry city with wide eyes.

It was more a mirage than a city.

The city wasn't real, but an illusion that sat at the top of the peak.

"I think it is," said Elvinia, her eyes burning with excitement. She had read some information about the Soul City, but this was the first time she was seeing it with her own eyes.

"But it's just an illusion," Zen said with a frown. What he was seeing was beyond his expectations.

"Not at all," said a Soul of Light from behind him.

The reason why they were able to come here so easily was because of Zen.

They didn't have anything with which to repay him, which was why they were willing to give out information they knew. The Soul of Light continued, "The Soul City itself is made up of souls. It is said that it sucked tens of millions of souls before becoming what it is now. So the city you see is similar to a Soul of Light."

"The city formed by Souls of Light is so huge!" Zen gasped, shocked.

A short while later, he and Elvinia passed through the long, winding path and reached the top of the peak. The blood fog that had followed him dissipated here.

The gate of the Soul City was huge and grayish brown.

Two gigantic square columns sat on both sides. When Zen walked to one of the columns, he could hear a moan emanating from within.

The square column itself was formed by Souls of Light. They could see dark brown masses within it floated ceaselessly, with many strange faces on them.

"Are these Souls of Light still alive?" Zen asked with surprise.

"Of course they are alive, but they are and will always be a part of the Soul City. They can't be reborn forever!" the Primeval Lord of Heaven's voice rang out.

"It looks like I have underestimated the Soul City," Zen muttered, growing serious.

The Soul City tested the Souls of Light. Only Indigo Souls at the ultimate level were qualified to enter the city. As it opened once every 132 hours, most of the Souls of Light would leave the Other Shore after arriving and would enter the city when its door opened.

Most of the Souls of Light that stayed at the entrance of the city hadn't reached the ultimate level of the Indigo Soul yet. They either sat crosslegged at the entrance and cultivated, or tried to collect enough soul crystal to strengthen themselves.

"Elvinia, wait for me here," said Zen.

Zen's physical body was here, but his Soul of Light was still in the lower stage. If he wanted to enter the Soul City, he had to come with his Soul of Light. Elvinia had a natural advantage over him since her physical body was just similar to an "armor" which protected her soul on the Other Shore.

It was not as troublesome as Zen's body. Now that he had sent Elvinia here, he had to bring his Soul of Light up.

Elvinia nodded in response and waited.

It took some time for Zen's Soul of Light to arrive here from the lower stage. Without the protection of his physical body, Zen's Soul of Light, which was at the ultimate level of the Indigo Soul, was relatively weak and he still had to pass through Stage Twenty-eight.

Fortunately, the Element Spirit race paid most of their attention to his physical body, which was why they didn't do a strict inspection of the Souls of Light. What was more, it wouldn't be easy for them to recognize Zen's Soul of Light.

After safely crossing Stage Twenty-eight, Zen quickly came to Stage Twenty-nine, the Constant Glory Stage. He used the Blood Fog Spell to move forward. It took him more than half a day of non-stop journey to finally appear at the entrance of the Soul City and meet Elvinia.

The two of them continued to wait at the gate of the Soul City. A day later, more and more Souls of Light appeared at the gate.

They included members of the Separate Abyss race, the Azure Wolf race, the New Moon race, and the human race.

Souls of Light of all races had emerged.

The previously quiet square in front of the Soul City became noisy almost instantly.

"To enter the Soul City, you need reach the ultimate level of the Indigo Soul. You will be courting death if you don't. I still have the soul crystal that I'm selling at a low price. Only three million soul pills per finger-size trunk." an Ear Mouse exclaimed, seizing the opportunity to sell its soul crystal.

Chapter 3713 The Soul Pillars A smile appeared on Zen's face when he heard the voice of the Ear Mouse hawking its soul crystal.

Normally, a finger-size chunk of soul crystal could be bought with one million soul pills. Now, however, these Ear Mice asked for three million.

Their greed was really insatiable.

Nevertheless, the Souls of Light crowding around the gate of the Soul City were in a hurry to pass the trial. If they really fell just a little short of the required level, they would most likely choose to pay three million soul pills.

Besides, the strong warriors who had reached this level must have a high status in their respective races, so they could afford so many soul pills.

After a while, the gate of the Soul City slowly opened.

The moment the gate opened, numerous faces of the Souls of Light appeared on the gate and let out incessant wails.

At the same time, a vast amount of soul auras flooded out of the city.

Zen had seen the auras of the Souls of Light of Eternal Realm masters, such as Eastern Emperor Taiyi and Emperor Charm. However, even the auras of Eternal Warriors could not be compared to those in front of him.

The Soul City was formed by trillions of souls after all.

"The gate is open!"

"I hope I can go further this time!"

"Every time I came, I always failed to move forward. I've been stuck in that step for years."

As soon as the gate was opened, it was immediately jammed with countless people trying to enter the city.

"Let's go in," said Zen.

He and Elvinia immediately followed the other Souls of Light into the Soul City.

The moment Zen set foot in the Soul City, he was immediately wrapped in the ubiquitous soul auras. Generally speaking, the soul aura could be seen as leaked consciousness, and consciousness itself could be said as one's deepest thought or desire. For example, when someone's desire to kill was strong, their soul aura would become extremely sharp, just like a sharpened knife.

A weak soul exposed to a murderous aura would feel very uncomfortable. If it was too weak, it would even be annihilated directly.

If it was a gentle aura, it could comfort the other party and even had the effect of repairing the soul.

There were countless souls in the Soul City, and each had their own consciousness, so the soul auras contained within were incomparably complicated. They had a very cumbersome impact on Zen.

He seemed to be able to listen to the thoughts of millions of people at the same time. Some of them were crying; some were drowned in sadness; some were feeling like outcasts; some were angry; some were bubbling with excitement; some others were filled with happiness.

Elvinia was also experiencing the same thing as Zen.

It was different from real hearing. Listening to these souls could not be gotten rid of, and they had to bear with it as long as they were in the Soul City. In fact, the test had already begun when they stepped into the Soul City.

Fortunately, Zen and Elvinia had already reached the ultimate level of the Indigo Soul, so their souls were strong and very stable.

Not far from them, a Soul of Light casually walked into the Soul City.

Before long, however, he staggered. The pressure of the complex soul auras gradually increased as he went farther into the city, and he couldn't endure it. He tried to cover his ears to escape from the auras but to no avail.

Once the auras became too overbearing to bear, he finally let out a scream and used all his strength to rush out of the Soul City. He managed to step out of the Soul City right as his soul power was exhausted, but he soon fell on the ground, dying.

Many people in the city noticed this scene, and most of them had pity in their gazes.

"That guy is so bold."

"How dare he come to the Soul City before reaching the ultimate level of the Indigo Soul? It's courting death!"

"Fortunately, he still had the brain to escape when he couldn't hold on any longer. Otherwise, he would've become a part of the Soul City!"

After they walked in the Soul City for some time, some pillars appeared in front of them. The pillars were only half a person tall, and they could climb up by leaping. One after another, those who walked in the front started to leap onto the pillars and then sat cross-legged.

When Zen was sizing the pillars up, Elvinia said, "These are the soul pillars.

Let's go up too."

"Soul pillars?" Zen repeated curiously.

"Yes, the test in the Soul City is completed on top of these soul pillars. As long as you pass this test, you will have a Colorless Soul and reach the Holy Soul Realm," said Elvinia.

She got this information after rummaging through a number of books. As for what exactly they would experience on the soul pillars, she actually didn't really know.

Zen nodded. After finding an unoccupied soul pillar, he gently jumped up and then sat down on top of it with his legs crossed. Elvinia found a soul pillar beside Zen's and did the same.

After everyone sat down, numbers appeared on the soul pillars. Both Elvinia's and Zen's soul pillars showed "one", while that of the Soul of Light on Zen's right side showed "sixty-three". A number above 1, 300 even appeared on an occupied soul pillar quite a distance away.

While Zen looked around, Elvinia said, "These numbers should represent how many times we've entered the Soul City. It's our first time, so our soul pillars show 'one'."

"The number on that pillar is more than 1, 300, so the Soul of Light sitting on it has entered the Soul City for more than 1, 000 times?" Zen asked.

"Exactly," Elvinia answered with a nod.

After Zen sat on the soul pillar, it gave no response. Nevertheless, more and more Souls of Light entered the Soul City, and some humans also entered in groups.

A group of about six or seven people walked towards Elvinia upon entering the area of the soul pillars.

"Princess Elvinia!" someone shouted.

Just like the creatures on the Other Shore, Elvinia had a physical body in the Soul City, so her presence was very conspicuous. The disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace naturally noticed her at a glance.

Elvinia looked at the Soul of Light and asked, "Who are you?"

"My name is Gabriel," the man replied.

"I'm Carver," another man introduced himself.

"I'm Libby," a woman said.

These people were all disciples from the third floor. They were quite famous in the Oneness Sky Palace. Elvinia had naturally seen them before, but she wasn't too familiar with them. Now that they introduced themselves like this, she naturally knew who they were.

Elvinia smiled and said, "What a coincidence. I guess I'll make a breakthrough to the Holy Soul Realm along with you guys."

Entering the Soul City and reaching the Holy Soul Realm was never an easy task.

It was an extremely painful test for souls. Some people gave up after trying several times, unwilling to take this test again for the rest of their lives.

Those who could come to the Soul City for hundreds or thousands of times were the persistent ones.

It was the first time Elvinia had entered the Soul City. In the eyes of others, she was a mere newcomer.

"Princess Elvinia, work hard," Gabriel encouraged.

Upon introducing herself, Libby looked at the soul pillar next to Elvinia's and asked, "Princess Elvinia, may I know who this man is?"

In fact, she already knew the answer. After the battle in the Oneness Sky Palace, she knew that Elvinia had a close relationship with Zen. The man who came to Stage Twenty-nine with Elvinia must be that powerful Zen.

"This is Zen," Elvinia replied curtly.

While Zen didn't return to the Land of Sword Grief after the battle with the Sun Crow race, the story of his deeds had undoubtedly spread to that place, turning him into a household name.

Before Goran went to the Dragon Cliff, he said in the Land of Sword Grief, "If it wasn't because our Oneness Sky Palace had Zen, the human race in the Bloom Divine Province would've been exterminated."

The significance of Zen's presence was self-evident.

Chapter 3714 Reading The Sanskrit Words Together with the other disciples of the third floor, Gabriel observed Zen's Soul of Light with utmost curiosity.

Considering Zen's Soul of Light alone, it might seem there was nothing absolutely remarkable about him.

After all, anyone who was able to enter the Soul City was obviously at the ultimate level of the Indigo Soul. People like Gabriel and Carver had been staying at this level for a long time.

Therefore, Zen and Elvinia who had just made it to Stage Twenty-nine were still considered as novices here.

However, Zen was a famous disciple of the Oneness Sky Palace. Almost everyone had heard of his name before.

Among the disciples in the entire Land of Sword Grief, Libby had seen the most of the battle against the Sun Crow race. Back then, she was a novice in the Oneness Array.

On the other hand, Gabriel and Carver only had the option to join the twelve passes and become Oneness Generals.

"It's a pleasure to meet you, Zen!"

"Nice to finally meet you!"

Gabriel, Carver, and the other disciples of the third floor all came forward, cupped their hands and bowed slightly as they greeted Zen. They all seemed too enthused.

With that, Zen also bowed slightly to them. "This is the very first time that Elvinia and I have entered the Soul City. Thus, we are very unfamiliar with this place. I hope you can lend us a hand," he said politely.

"No problem! It is safe to say that with your strength, it won't be that difficult to pass the test of the Soul City," replied Gabriel with a reassuring smile.

"Is that so? Well, that is quite flattering." Zen humbly accepted the compliment with a wave of his hand.

All of a sudden, his soul pillar flashed and began to vibrate slightly while he was still speaking.

Carver noticed this as well. So he said, "The soul pillars are about to ascend. Come, let's choose our own pillars!"

There were lots of soul pillars all over the entire Soul City. Many of the ones located behind Zen were not occupied. With a gentle leap, Carver, Gabriel, and the other disciples skillfully boarded the soul pillars and sat down cross legged.

The number on Libby's soul pillar was seventeen. This meant that she had already come to the Soul City for the seventeenth time. Carver's number was one hundred and ninety-eight, while Gabriel's was two hundred and thirty. The two of them had been to the Soul City many times before.

"With Zen's strength, it'll be very easy for him to pass the test of the Soul City, right?" Carver whispered to Gabriel.

Gabriel merely snorted at this. "As far as I know, he did not gain those great achievements in the battle against the Sun Crows because of his own strength. He only attained them because he received lots of help from some supreme masters!"

Being disciples on the third floor of the Land of Sword Grief, Gabriel and Carver felt extremely proud of themselves. Libby was the only person they admired within the entire place.

To be honest, they were quite uncomfortable with Zen's arrival.

Gabriel was the son of the Bright Mountain's leader. His father's death was a great blow to him. Needless to say, he did everything in his power to investigate what happened to his father. Therefore, he knew more about Zen's deeds than ordinary people.

"I see. It really was quite unthinkable that a man who didn't even pass the test of the Soul City could stand against the mighty warriors of the Sun Crow race. All of the people in the Oneness Sky Palace have even admired him as if he was a God. This will be too much for him," Carver said.

"Well, it's his first time to sit on the soul pillar. Judging from the looks of it, he doesn't even know what kind of test he is going to face. It'll be fun watching him make a fool of himself later." Gabriel smirked mockingly.

At this very moment, the soul pillars trembled once again. Slowly, they began to rise.

The soul pillar that Zen had sat on was rising as well. It gradually ascended by ten feet, twenty feet, thirty feet...

As soon as the soul pillars rose, a brown cloud started to press down from above the Soul City. The cloud seemed to contain a mix of countless souls and innumerable twisted faces that struggled and howled inside it.

The soul cloud continued pressing down as the soul pillars went up. The soul pressure became more and more intense as Zen continued to approach the cloud.

"Could this be the test of the Soul City?" Zen mumbled to himself with a frown.

He wondered whether merely dealing with the soul pressure was enough to strengthen one's own Soul of Light.

From the moment Zen began to cultivate his soul, he had felt no change yet.

Everyone's soul had reached a limit after reaching the ultimate level of the Indigo Soul. Even if they absorbed more soul crystal, they still wouldn't be able to advance to a higher level.

Therefore, Zen didn't believe that the test of the Soul City was to just deal with the soul pressure. There had to be a different trial hidden behind this.

The soul pillars had now ascended to fifty feet.

They rose to a hundred feet while the pressure kept rising.

Zen noticed that they were now nearing two hundred feet.

As soon as the soul pillars reached two hundred feet, they stopped. The soul cloud above also stopped descending. It hovered just ten feet away from all of the Souls of Light.

At this close distance, Zen could observe the soul cloud more clearly.

There were all sorts of strange faces and some sharp tiny crystals swirling within the cloud. These tiny crystals were the ones that reflected colorful lights from the soul cloud.

What were they supposed to do now? Were they going to enter the soul cloud? All of a sudden, they heard strange sounds coming from within the cloud just as Zen was pondering about what their next move should be.

At first, they sounded like unintelligible screams. However, they started to become even more peculiar now.

After listening to them for a while, Zen noticed something. The tones and pronunciation of the screams were becoming intensely rhythmic. Now, they sounded like a pleasant song! "Wait a second. It's a song?" Zen gazed at the cloud intently. His face registered a look of astonishment.

Realizing this, it gave him an utterly bizarre feeling. It felt like the cloud had taken the form of a young girl who was singing. However, this young girl didn't have a mouth so obviously, she wouldn't be able to sing.

Therefore, she was using the mouths of the souls in the cloud. She created a song by gathering lots of different sounds together.

At this point, the voice of the Primeval Lord of Heaven rang clearly once again. "Listen carefully, Zen. This song contains the comprehension of the Colorless Soul."

"The comprehension of the Colorless Soul is in the song?" Zen repeated as he stared incredulously at the soul cloud. "What shall I do? I can't understand it at all." Zen was evidently stunned.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven looked at him and smiled. "Well, do you understand Sanskrit words?"

Unfortunately, Zen couldn't understand Sanskrit words either. He didn't have the incredible ability to decipher the Sanskrit words instantly just like Geoffrey. If he truly wanted to decipher the Sanskrit words methodically, it would definitely take him a very long time.

Coming out of his reverie, Zen had a sudden realization. "Do you mean to say that this song..." His voice trailed away as he waited for the answer.

"Yes, these are their voices." The Primeval Lord of Heaven confirmed what Zen had on his mind.

It was well-known that Sanskrit words were incomprehensible within the chaos.

If people really wanted to read and understand them, they had to decipher them first. However, this method was time-consuming.

Meanwhile, Geoffrey had merely translated the Sanskrit words without even knowing how to read them.

In actuality, Sanskrit words could be read. However, there wasn't a single person in the chaos who could read Sanskrit words instantly.

"It turns out those Sanskrit words are read in such a strange and baffling way," Zen mused. He tilted his head to the side and listened carefully.

Based on his observation, there were times when the sounds were rising and falling in cadence and then suddenly becoming delicate and subtle. To him, they seemed like a poem or a song. They were like people scolding each other in the marketplace. They could only be understood mentally.

Therefore, they could not be described by mere words.

After listening closely for a while, Zen smiled bitterly. "How will I be able to cultivate the Colorless Soul and reach the Holy Soul Realm with this? I can't quite make sense of these chaotic and irregular sounds."

Chapter 3715 One Thousand Feet To Pass The Test "Listen carefully," the Primeval Lord of Heaven muttered in an urgent tone.

"Back then, I only entered Soul City three times before I was able to pass through. I was able to do that because of my comprehension of this song."

Zen's eyes widened in astonishment. "You were able to pass through after just three tries?"

The Primeval Lord of Heaven beamed with pride. "Of course!"

It was not difficult to pass the Soul City's test, but that didn't mean it was easy either. After all, only those who were able to reach Stage Twenty-nine of the Other Shore were able to enter the Soul City, which meant they had to have a certain level of talent and skill to be qualified.

Every third-floor disciple of the Land of Sword Grief like Gabriel, Carver, or Libby would also be considered a favored talent had they been part of any other super force in the Source World.

So long as they worked hard and tried their best, they would eventually pass the Soul City's test. The only variation was the length of time it took for them to succeed.

The fastest person in history to have passed through Soul City was the Grandmaster of Heaven, who was the Primeval Lord of Heaven's junior fellow disciple.

The two of them had entered the Soul City for the first time on the same day. The Primeval Lord of Heaven passed after three tries while the Grandmaster of Heaven was able to do it after two. This was the main reason why the Primeval Lord of Heaven always thought his fellow disciple was way more talented than him.

Their records remained unbroken even now.

The song lingered in Zen's ears and he no longer cared whether he understood the lyrics or not. Instead, he chose to close his eyes and listened closely.

Elvinia was also listening with a serene expression on her face as she sat cross-legged on another pillar.

Whilst everyone listened, a soul pillar began to rise. On top of this pillar was a member of the Separate Abyss race.

This Separate Abyss member had a big build and looked somewhat funny on top of the pillar because of it. He had to carefully maintain his balance in order not to fall off.

Since he was the first to enter the soul cloud, everyone's attention was on him.

"That's Toby from the Separate Abyss race!"

"He is ascending so fast! Is he determined to pass the test this time?"

"Of course he is! He's already tried for more than one thousand three hundred times, right?" "Toby was a very promising member of the Separate Abyss race, but he's been stuck in Soul City for quite a while. His other race members laugh at him because he can't pass the test and the only way he'd get his prestige back is if he succeeds and passes through."

Zen's eyes also fell on the soul pillar as he heard everyone's discussion. As they said, the number displayed on the soul pillar was over one thousand three hundred.

As the soul pillar rose, Toby got closer and closer to the cloud. He let out a growl before finally entering it.

Numerous faces in the cloud rotated around the vortex where he entered.

As Toby disappeared into the soul cloud, another number showed up on his soul pillar.

Zen didn't need any explanation from Elvinia. He quickly understood that this new number indicated the height Toby was at in the soul cloud.

It seemed that after entering the soul cloud, Toby was able to rise in one go.

Meanwhile, the number on the soul pillar continued to increase.

Ten feet...

Twenty feet...

Thirty feet...

Though it seemed as if his speed was slow, in the eyes of the Souls of Light in the Soul City, this feat was already impressive.

"Toby has indeed made progress!"

"He spent three seconds less on the first one hundred feet than last time!"

"It seems that the Separate Abyss race will be gaining one more powerful warrior in the thirty-second stage of the Other Shore Realm!"

It was a significant feat for one's Soul of Light to reach Stage Thirty-two of the Other Shore, but there was no way a warrior would be able to become an Eternal Warrior due to the absence of a corporeal body.

Flamine, Athemar, and Goran all fell into this category.

Nevertheless, nobody really hoped to become an Eternal Warrior. Everyone knew it was an impossible dream in this era.

One hundred feet...

Two hundred feet...

Five hundred feet...

The moment just before someone passed the test always garnered the most attention.

After all, the Soul City opened every few days and not that many people were eager to pass the test. During times like this, everyone focused on one specific warrior to see if he'd be able to succeed.

Not long after, the number on Toby's soul pillar broke through the nine hundred feet mark.

Nine hundred and fifty feet...

Nine hundred and sixty feet...

Nine hundred and seventy feet...

Nine hundred and eighty feet...

"He's about to reach nine hundred and ninety feet!"

"Last time he got to around nine hundred and eighty feet. There's only ten feet left!"

"Nine hundred and ninety! He's reached nine-hundred and ninety! Only ten feet left!"

Toby only needed ten more feet to reach his goal of achieving the Colorless Soul! Just as everyone waited in bated breath for the number to reach one thousand feet, the soul pillar shook.

"Whoosh!"

They watched as a figure, thirty feet tall, came crashing down through the soul cloud, and slammed heavily onto the ground.

Toby had failed yet again.

There was a series of disappointed sighs as they looked at his unmoving form.

"Alas, he was so close..."

"He reached nine hundred and ninety-five feet! He was so close!"

"Only five feet left, what a pity! He can only try again next time..."

Whenever the test started, everyone would be given only one chance to ascend. There was no getting back on a soul pillar to try again for that round.

The defeated Toby slowly got up and leaned against the soul pillar and cast a silent but sad look at the soul cloud above him.

He had failed for more than one thousand times, but he took it in stride.

Toby knew his own strength and that there was no way he'd be able to rise even half a foot more when he was up there. He'd have to work on himself more to pass the test sooner or later.

After Toby's initial failure, a few other Souls of Light began to drive their soul pillars up through the cloud. Others still eagerly listened to the song in hopes of an epiphany.

"There's no need to be nervous for your first try, Zen. Everyone fails the first time," Gabriel assured Zen.

Carver echoed his sentiment. "Yes. There's no need to be nervous. Besides, even if this is your first time I don't doubt for a second that your performance will be extraordinary!"

Being in the soul cloud wasn't a walk in the park. If one was not wellprepared, then he or she could end up in a miserable state.

Hearing their words, Elvinia, who had been listening attentively to the song, opened her eyes and gave them a frown.

She was just about to refute what they said when a voice suddenly spoke.

"Gabriel, Carver, what nonsense are you two spouting?!"

It was Libby. She turned to Zen and began to give him tips and warnings.

"Zen, the cloud is full of dangers. Don't be careless. You can't enter the soul cloud until you've comprehended the song to a certain degree. If you feel uncomfortable at any point, you can jump down. It won't matter if you fail.

Just don't ever force yourself to hold on!"

Libby's scolding was effective in zipping Gabriel's and Carver's mouths into silence.

Zen nodded in understanding at her warning and continued to listen to the song.

At the same time, Libby's soul pillar began to rise and send her up into the soul cloud.

It was only her seventeenth time here in the Soul City but the speed at which she rose was remarkable owing to her outstanding ability of comprehension.

Chapter 3716 The Holy Soul Imprint The last time she entered the Soul City, Libby had risen to a height of six hundred and twenty feet.

It was only her sixteenth time entering the Soul City, so being able to reach such a height was a big deal in the city. There were very few people like her, at least in the Source World. Naturally, she attracted a lot of attention in the Soul City.

Libby's rising speed was far from Toby's. She was careful the entire time, rising at a constant speed. Within five minutes, she had risen over a hundred feet.

After a few minutes, she was at six hundred feet.

Gabriel, Carver, and the rest paid close attention to Libby, nervously watching her soul pillar.

"This time, she may rise to a height of over seven hundred feet!"

"Maybe she can break the Oneness Sky Palace's record!"

"Look, she's broken her last record!"

After reaching the height of six hundred and twenty feet, Libby continued to rise. While she was somewhat slowing down, she still rose steadily and constantly.

When the soul pillar reached a height of seven hundred feet, it finally came to a stop.

Whoosh! A shadow descended from the soul cloud quickly, steadily landing on the ground.

Just as Libby had said to Zen, she never forced herself in the soul cloud. It was only natural that she wasn't as miserable as Toby when she landed.

"Libby, you've reached a height of seven hundred feet at the seventeenth attempt. You truly are the pride of our Oneness Sky Palace!" praised Gabriel.

"I'm flattered," Libby said flatly.

After all, she never gave much importance to the records; otherwise, she could have pushed her abilities further.

Just as the people of the Land of Sword Grief complimented her, an emotionless voice came from nearby. "The Oneness Sky Palace is proud of seven hundred feet? Interesting."

Everyone turned to the source of the voice. Standing on the soul pillar was a human Soul of Light. The soul pillar displayed the number eleven.

This indicated that the person had entered the Soul City eleven times.

"It's Dailey Ji from the Bearing race!"

"He is said to be the strongest talent of the Bearing race since its beginnings, someone with talent greater than the Yellow Thearch's!"

"It's said that the first time he entered the Soul City, he had risen to a height of seven hundred and ninety feet. At his tenth time, he's already reached nine hundred and fifty feet."

Regardless of what race they belonged to, so long as they were geniuses, they'd always attract much attention.

Dailey's words immediately attracted the Souls of Light's attention. He was the topic of conversation for both the human race and the other races in the Source World.

"What's the big deal? You haven't even reached a thousand feet yet. Even if you reach nine hundred and ninety feet, it's no different from ten. Before daring to mock it, you must go through the Soul City first," Gabriel retorted coldly.

Daily threw him an indifferent glance—he looked down upon the latter, someone who had entered the Soul City over two hundred times.

"One thousand feet?" With a faint smile, Dailey said, "It's easy to achieve the Colorless Soul. What I pursue is nothing like what you do. You don't understand anything!"

At that, Gabriel, Carver, and the non-human creatures were all left confused.

Those who entered the Soul City all pursued the Colorless Soul and the Holy Soul Realm. What else was Dailey pursuing? "Look, everyone, and the pride of the Oneness Sky Palace," Dailey called out with a smile as the soul pillar under his feet began to rise.

The pillar rose rapidly, as did its number.

One hundred feet.

Two hundred feet.

Three hundred feet.

In about thirty seconds, Dailey had risen to a height of over eight hundred feet before going straight to nine hundred.

"That is fast!"

"The soul cloud imposes no hindrance to him whatsoever…"

"It seems he can pass through the Soul City this time…"

Before the speaker could finish speaking, the number on Dailey's soul pillar revealed one thousand.

"Buzz..."

When the number appeared, the entire dense soul cloud began emitting a faint light, indicating that Dailey had passed.

"I knew he could do it fast!"

"I'm so jealous. He can safely pass the Soul City and go to the upper stage on the Other Shore now."

"Eh? Wait, look..."

Normally, so long as people reached a thousand feet, they would be relieved before jumping down from their soul pillars. It was meaningless to remain there or continue going beyond the finish line, after all.

But as everyone gazed upon him, Dailey did not leave. Instead, he continued rising just as the number on the soul pillar continued increasing.

"What does Dailey want to do?"

"He wants to make a name for himself in the Soul City?"

"No, I heard a stronger level lies above the Holy Soul Realm, so long as we have the ability to continue to advance."

From the soul cloud, a light shot into the sky. Dailey sat upright on the soul pillar as he rushed out of the soul cloud and continued rising in the light.

"Primeval Lord of Heaven, isn't the limit of the Soul City a thousand feet?"

Zen asked, looking at Dailey.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven chuckled and said, "For the vast majority of people, it's indeed a thousand feet. Crossing this height means one will obtain a Colorless Soul and reach the Holy Soul Realm. But do you remember I told you that the Holy Soul Realm is not the end?"

Zen nodded. He had indeed told him when they first met.

"When one achieves the Colorless Soul, they will have a chance to try and reach a higher level. There is only one chance of this. If one misses it, there will be no second chance. But most of them choose to give up because moving forward proves to be too difficult," the Primeval Lord of Heaven said, looking at Dailey who was above the soul cloud. "He is an outstanding warrior of perception. He should be able to obtain a Holy Soul Imprint."

"A Holy Soul Imprint?" Zen asked, raising his brows.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven nodded. "One imprint should be his limit."

Having already reached a thousand feet, Dailey found it difficult to go further.

The fact was now obvious to most.

While Dailey was indeed extraordinary, it wasn't easy for him to move upward in the light, let alone quickly.

An hour later, he had risen up to eighty feet, with the soul pillar showing a thousand and eighty feet.

Buzz! A golden imprint circled Dailey, attaching itself to the very surface of his soul. He then jumped down from the soul pillar and fell hard to the ground.

Although the crowd couldn't see Dailey's face clearly, they could still feel his great joy.

When he entered the Soul City for the eighth time, he already had the confidence to rise up to a thousand feet. For so long, he had prepared to reach his goal of the Holy Soul Imprint.

Chapter 3717 Nine Holy Soul Imprints Everyone stopped whatever they were doing, stunned by what just happened to Dailey.

Most of them were clueless of the Holy Soul Imprint to begin with.

When ordinary people reached one thousand feet, they would have met the end of their ropes. At this height, they wouldn't be able to hold on long, and their soul pillars wouldn't rise any more.

However, the world always had extraordinary warriors.

In the past, people already discovered that one thousand feet was not the farthest they could go. Once this height was met, the soul pillar could still rise if one possessed enough strength.

Meanwhile, there were a handful of creatures with extraordinary talents who attempted to push the envelope. Though one person would only have one chance, some of them finally obtained the Holy Soul Imprints.

"I can't believe that Dailey obtained a Holy Soul Imprint!"

"He truly is so great!"

"Wow, and it's been so long since I saw someone do that last time..."

People started chattering about Dailey's success.

Because those who were qualified to obtain a Holy Soul Imprint were so few, ordinary people forgot about it. Seeing Dailey do it, everyone was reminded about the imprint and in turn, shocked them.

As Dailey studied the Holy Soul Imprint on his chest, the corners of his lips turned up for a small smile.

"Congratulations, Dailey!"

"Another member of the Bearing race successfully obtained a Holy Soul Imprint!"

"Dailey, you surely have a bright future ahead of you!"

Just then, the Soul of Lights from the Bearing race also came up to congratulate him.

However, Libby stood a few meters away, looking not so pleased.

In the Oneness Sky Palace, she was the apple of everyone's eye, but in the Source World, she was not significant at all.

It was for this reason that she knew Dailey was a lot stronger than her in everything.

"Big deal."

Gabriel snorted, annoyed with the situation. He sat on his soul pillar, which was found deep into the soul cloud. Behind him followed Carver, who rose into the cloud very gracefully.

"Anson has been eaten by that big fish!" Toby roared.

The others of the Separate Abyss race all cried in horror as well.

It was then that the door to Soul City shut completely with a monstrous bang.

Chapter 3722 Dreaded Eyes Each time the gates to the Soul City were closed, the souls imprisoned in the walls and the earth would emerge in a bloodthirsty haze.

Because they had no consciousness, their only instinct was to constantly devour or be devoured. There were no winners here.

Even the most powerful of souls would eventually exhaust its energy, and turn into a mindless zombie till it sank back into the earth and became a part of the Soul City.

After a while, they would be born once more, and began to devour other souls to grow more powerful, until they sank back into the earth, and so on.

The cycle was never ending.

The Souls of Light from the Source World often waited outside the Soul City. From the gates, they could hear all kinds of howls and shrieks coming from within the Soul City.

The Soul City was not home to Souls of Light nor the Other Shore creatures. It was home to these resentful souls.

Now that the door was closed and all the Souls of Light were locked inside, it was not hard to imagine how things would turn out for them.

"Everyone, huddle!"

Libby reacted quickly and ordered with a trace of anxiety in her voice.

In a situation this chaotic, if they tried to fight on their own, it was only a matter of time before they all died. Now, they needed to band closely together.

However, when the swords hit the surface the dragon-shaped soul, the energy actually bounced off and disappeared into thin air.

Libby's face fell. Trembling slightly, she felt an incredible need to run away.

However, the dragon-shaped soul was extremely fast. It bared its menacing teeth at Libby, poised to bite her head off.

Just as she was about to shut her eyes tight, a figure flashed in front of her.

"Boom!"

After locking onto its target, the fish-shaped soul suddenly jumped up from the ground, like a salmon leaping gracefully into the air from a river.

Despite chances of survival looking quite slim, the Souls of Light continued to launch their counterattacks. However, those light golden souls were not willing to give up. They wandered in the ground and observed carefully. As long as there was a chance, they would jump up, tear up a Soul of Light, swallow it into their mouths, and then dive into the ground...

In the cabin, from the small window, Zen could see the chaos taking place outside. His expression darkened.

All these strange things started happening only after the golden pot fell to the ground, extinguishing the flame.

It didn't take a genius to figure out the cause and effect.

The Soul City would open every 132 hours. When it opened, the window of the cabin would be illuminated. Evidently, this was thanks to the flame of the golden pot.

In other words, every 132 hours, the golden pot would automatically light up with a flame--or, someone lit it every 132 hours.

Once the flame was ignited, the doors to the Soul City would open.

Then, 132 hours later, the flame of the golden pot would be extinguished, closing the gates to the Soul City.

Now that the flame was extinguished by Zen, the door closed in advance! Just seconds after flame was extinguished, the Soul City was already in chaos. Zen needed to ignite the flame again somehow.

"Flame..."

When Zen was in the form of his physical body, he could use the Elementary Fire Godly Way to easily release flames.

But in this situation, where could he possibly find a fire? Anxiously, he racked his brains trying to come up with a solution.

Suddenly, his eyes lit up and he turned to the Primeval Lord of Heaven. "Is Master Zhurong able to..."

Before he could even finish speaking, the Primeval Lord of Heaven replied.

"If Zhurong can make a move, I can also release flames to help you ignite the golden pot. But you have forgotten what form you are in now."

The Civilization Artifacts were borne by Zen's inner world, turning into a strange form. When Zen entered the Other Shore with his physical body, he could release them from his inner world.

However, when he was in the form of Soul of Light, he couldn't use any Godly Way. Consequently, the Primeval Lord of Heaven and the others wouldn't be able to help much.

Zen's frown deepened and he turned to stare outside the window again.

Suddenly, a streak of golden lightning flashed across the soul cloud.

"Crack!"

Two huge dark blue eyes emerged from the depths of the soul cloud.

Chapter 3723 The Second Hand Many soul hunters with strange shapes and peculiar figures had already emerged from the soul cloud.

These hunters moved at an incredibly high speed all over the place. They moved on the ground, on the walls, and along the surface of the soul pillars.

In despair, she suddenly thought of her right hand! Chapter 3724 A Cold Civilization When they were in Stage Thirteen of the Other Shore, Elvinia had given all the things stored inside her Sumeru space back to Zen.

Chapter 3725 Starry Roc-fish The Snake Goddess, Fuxi and the others all agreed with the Primeval Lord of Heaven's conclusion.

The others didn't think it was that simple. If the Instant Civilization really looked down upon the later "bug"-like ruling civilizations that would come, they would not have made all kinds of complex rules on the Other Shore.

For example, the suppressive power of every stage of the Other Shore was different. If this rule was removed, the Element Spirit Civilization that had set foot on the Other Shore first, would probably have dominated the entire Other Shore and anyone who came after wouldn't have stood a chance.

The Instant Civilization would not create such a meticulous and painstaking blueprint if they saw the future generations as bugs...

Stage Thirty-three is at the top of the chaos, then if we look up, what we see above our heads should be the ceiling, right?"

Chapter 3726 Return There was only one picture within the cabin. A wisp of flame was gracefully depicted on the Starry Roc-fish.
