Dorothy blinked in uneasiness, her heartbeat quickening, and she asked, "What about the door on the right?"

"That door leads to Stage Thirty-three of the Other Shore," the white-haired monster replied.

Dorothy narrowed her eyes on hearing this.

Upon learning her grandmother was in danger, she wanted little else other than to enter Stage Thirty-three of the Other Shore.

But she knew this was impossible for her.

She first had to become an Eternal Warrior and she might never even achieve that.

All her hopes were now placed on that door.

She did not expect there to actually be a path leading to Stage Thirty-three of the Other Shore.

"If I want to step into Stage Thirty-three, I must become an Eternal Warrior and reach the Eternal Realm. Can I do that in my current state?" Dorothy asked.

"Of course not." The white-haired monster laughed.

"You do not want to go home, you want to go to Stage Thirty-three of the Other Shore?" The long-haired monster asked, hovering behind Dorothy as she looked forward down the passageway.

Dorothy was their race's only hope.

Just now, the long-haired monster and the white-haired monster had discussed whether they should tell her the way home.

If they told her, would she move on and leave them behind? Should they explain to her what had happened in that world? What if she insisted on doing as she pleased? They had prepared a detailed explanation, but it seemed that Dorothy was not interested in the way home at all! And so the long-haired monster couldn't help but ask her that question.

"I have to go to Stage Thirty-three of the Other Shore," Dorothy replied firmly.

The long-haired monster and the white-haired monster looked at each other, their eyes twinkling with surprise.

If she wanted to remove the curse, she would also have to go to Stage Thirty-three of the Other Shore.

No matter what Dorothy's purpose was, at least she was headed in the same direction as them! "It is true that in your current state, you are unable to step into Stage Thirtythree, but I have a way to get you in," said the long-haired monster. "But you have to tell me your purpose of going there."

"To save my grandmother!" Dorothy blurted out.

The long-haired monster nodded. "We can help you with this matter, but we ask that you please keep your previous promise."

"To help you remove the curse?" Dorothy inquired.

"Yes."

Dorothy had already made up her mind as she walked down the passageway.

Her current fate seemed to have been determined in her previous life. She had no other choice but to fulfill that promise.

She would not refuse these monsters' requests.

Now they revealed they could help her save her grandmother in Stage Thirty-three of the Other Shore! If they really could help her, she would risk her life if she had to. She would obviously not hesitate to agree with them.

In the Crane Blood Province The Star Crane City was the most prosperous city of the Bearing race.

Three ancient towers were like pillars stretching out of the city to the sky.

Each ancient tower had thousands of floors, and housed the core disciples of the Bearing race. The Ji Clan was located in the Supreme Memorial Tower, between the other two towers.

Two hundred Other Shore Realm warriors had lined up on the capacious top floor of the Supreme Memorial Tower.

The Ji Clan had posted a notice some time ago, announcing they planned to select some strong Other Shore Realm warriors to join the Yellow Emperor Guards.

This was an excellent opportunity for the Other Shore Realm warriors scattered among the ordinary citizens to show their potential.

Joining the Yellow Emperor Guards would mean obtaining better resources and even some powerful Other Shore Tokens! Naturally, since the notice had been posted, more and more warriors flooded this place with hopes of becoming a Yellow Emperor Guard.

But now, their faces filled with confusion as they began muttering to themselves...

They were unsure of the reason for their being sent here. This was the headquarters of the Ji Clan, a place that was difficult for even the most powerful warriors in the Crane Blood Province to enter.

A huge gap existed between the Ji Clan and ordinary people.

Why would the warriors who applied to be one of the Yellow Emperor Guards be sent here? "Enter!"

The guards escorted the warriors into a palace.

A moment ago, they had smelled the faint scent of the wood in the corridor, but that was replaced with a strong smell of blood after they entered the palace, so strong that some almost passed out.

After they had entered, they saw a young man with black hair curl up in the corner of the palace.

He was naked, covered in blood, and his eyes flashed with a fierce light.

When the Other Shore Realm warriors saw him, they were instantly overtaken with a sense of foreboding.

Some wished to retreat...

Some wondered what was going on...

Suddenly, the door closed behind them and the guards shouted, "If you kill that young man, you qualify to join the Yellow Emperor Guards!"

"That young man doesn't appear to have even reached the Other Shore Realm!"

"He is at most a consummate True God. He can't even possess the power of one divine megaton."

"I will kill him!"

It was obvious how big the gap between the Other Shore Realm warrior and the True God was.

Such a large gap dispelled the fear in some hearts.

Others still kept a cool and collected head, not getting ahead of themselves.

If killing this man was easy, why were two hundred Other Shore Realm warriors sent here all at once? Those who recognized something was not quite as it seemed retreated to the corner, and some even looked for ways to escape...

But with the means of the Ji Clan, how would the mere Other Shore Realm warriors be able to escape? The black-haired boy stood up and a sinister aura began filling every corner of the room. Then, like a wolf ravaging a flock of sheep, he pounced on the crowd! Streams of blood spurted and sprayed on every wall as the warriors were ruthlessly killed.

Chapter 3737 Use Him It only took him five whole minutes to slaughter the two hundred warriors at the Other Shore Realm.

If that was not impressive enough, he was able to kill one hundred and ninety-eight of them in two minutes.

The rest were a bit difficult to get rid of because they resisted with their Other Shore Tokens. It came to a point that one of them transformed into a cloud of black fog, so naturally, his body couldn't be torn to pieces.

On the other hand, the remaining man used his Other Shore Token to open a box space and hid himself within.

Though the methods of these two were unique and effective, they did not last long. Eventually, the boy still dealt with them and killed them without breaking a sweat.

Pah! Pah! Pah! As soon as the boy was finished with the last man standing, a round of applause roared from the other end of the hall.

It was a woman in a white fox-fur robe, looking beautiful, dignified, and powerful.

"You've made rapid progress," that woman said.

The black-haired boy squinted his eyes and a darkness flashed behind his eyes. Suddenly, he propped his hands to the ground as if he were a beast, and pounced on the woman without hesitation.

Though it made him look primitive, the killing intent was definitely aggressive. There was no way the ordinary warriors at the Other Shore Realm could avoid this! The woman, however, just cocked her head and grabbed the boy by the arm, completely unthreatened.

Whoosh! With one swing, she tossed him away as if with little effort. Her one move contained about eight thousand divine megatons of force! Bang! Just like that, the black-haired boy was sent into the sky and slammed right into the wall.

The towering Supreme Memorial Tower let out a little shake in reaction to the impact.

The woman scoffed, "But no matter how much you have progressed, you are still no match to me now."

As she turned around to speak, the boy did not hesitate to pounce on her for the second time.

This time, her eyebrows were raised, surprised to see how confident the boy was. Like the first time, she grabbed him by the hair and lifted him off the ground. Left and right, she smashed the boy with no mercy whatsoever.

Boom! The force sent cracks into the arrays that protected the ground, and the boy was unmoving.

Still holding him by the head, the woman dragged him to the other side of the room. They entered the transmission door which transported them to an underground hall.

A strange stone was positioned at the center of the hall.

It appeared large, like a huge heart, but it was stronger and sturdier than anything else.

A line of warriors surrounded the stone, all of them having reached the Holy Soul Realm. They were the elites - the very foundation of the Bearing race.

A young man in a brocade robe chuckled at the sight of the woman. "You taught him a lesson again?"

The woman, on the other hand, couldn't help but sigh with resignation. "He won't give up until he is killed..."

"It's good that he can be subdued now," the man in brocade robe continued.

"However, when he becomes as strong as Usman, I'm afraid he will become a scourge to us." The man seemed worried, but tried his best not to let it overcome him.

In the past, Usman's behaviors had attracted the attention of all the super forces.

Usman was a very special, rare being. Unlike most warriors at the Other Shore Realm, he did not need to rely on the Other Shore Tokens. More than that, he did not seek the protection of the Chaotic Source Spirits when in battle. For some reason, his physical body and evil soul grew so much that he could even go up against the Eternal Warriors without fail! His way of growth was so unique that it caught the eye of many forces, and even made them jealous of the Black Ship.

However, his betrayal completely shifted his appearance to the super forces.

Filled with so many negative emotions and intentions, Usman was an ungrateful man. It was because of this that he grew to become an extremely evil existence, one that could never submit to anyone.

Once Yellow Thearch took the black-haired boy back, it worried the masters. They saw his frightening potential to follow in the footsteps of Usman.

However, because the strength of the black-haired boy was still weak and immature, he could still be watched and controlled.

If he continually grew at immense speed, it wouldn't be long until even Yellow Thearch found it difficult to suppress him.

"We are mere executors," the woman spoke out, dignified. "As for the consequences, I believe the emperor might have his own plans..."

Without any trace of gentleness, she dragged the boy and lifted him onto the heart-like stone.

Just as the boy made contact with the heart-like stone, it made a "plop"

sound.

It seemed that this heart-like stone suddenly throbbed.

The stone did not move, but it had a powerful sound or vibration from within it.

Plop! Plop! Plop! A few seconds had passed and the black-haired boy gradually fell asleep.

In his sleep, his bones extended, his hair grew, and he inched taller and taller by the minute.

However, everyone watching was not at all surprised.

They knew very well of the effects of the stone.

Plop...

From a boy with the body of an eight-year-old, the boy had the body of a fourteen-year-old within a few minutes.

"Look! He's about to wake up," the young man nudged the people around him.

"He's definitely going to cause some trouble," he added.

Though a few people were worried, the woman did not seem threatened.

The black-haired boy's eyes fluttered and eventually, opened. As the woman prepared to pin him down, he ended up not moving at all. He only lay on the stone, and then looked up to the sky.

It was as if he saw something that no one else had seen.

Surprised with his calmness, the woman and the young man looked at the scene and blinked their eyes in confusion.

Soon, a space fluctuation came from the left side of the hall.

From it, powerful cultivators at Holy Soul Realm walked out of the channel, and the last one to enter was a middle-aged man with sharp eyes.

"Your Majesty!"

At the sight of Yellow Thearch, all warriors immediately knelt down and bowed.

But Yellow Thearch seemed a bit anxious. He waved his hand to signal everyone to stand. They all made their way towards the side of the blackhaired boy.

Just then, Yellow Thearch reached out and gently put his palm against the boy's forehead, then looked up into the sky.

And though they were all underground, he saw through the ceiling almost immediately.

Under the scorching sun, a space was violently reverberating. It was as if something powerful was going to emerge.

This lasted for only a few seconds, until Yellow Thearch looked back down.

The boy's expression returned to normal as well.

Meanwhile, the emperor's face lit up as he scanned through the room and looked at the officials who were giving him expressions of worry.

He smiled. "What are you all so worried about?"

"Your Majesty, it's just that this child is the same as Usman. He can't be tamed. Are we..." The young man in brocade robe responded anxiously.

But before the young man could even finish his words, Yellow Thearch let up a hand and asked him to stop. "While it is true that Usman can't be tamed, I did not intend to treat him as a member in the first place."

"Your Majesty, have you found a way to control him?" The young man asked again.

But Yellow Thearch shook his head. "I just want to use him to control this world..."

There was a great connection between Usman and the entire Source World.

However, the connection remained hidden and undetectable despite the many efforts to find it.

But the situation had changed now.

With the guidance of the Element Spirit Civilization, he possessed a decent understanding of primitive land that could help them dig out useful information and resources.

Chapter 3738 To The Blooming Jade Stage The raven-haired boy's face remained dull and stiff for over an hour.

During this time, the fluctuation within the Source World quietly disappeared.

When the boy came back to his senses, he jumped off the stone—his instinct was to run away.

But too many powerful warriors were currently in the underground hall— any one of them could easily subdue him.

Before he could even take another step forward, he was trapped in an invisible cage.

Yellow Thearch walked briskly toward the raven-haired boy.

He figured that the boy would quickly get all memories of Usman, but he was surprised to find otherwise.

While the boy reacted to the mention of Usman, he didn't remember much about him.

Yellow Thearch felt a tremor between his brows before he could say something.

His face seemed to shift in color before he turned to the woman in white fox-fur robe.

"Take him back…"

The latter merely nodded and dragged the boy away.

Taking a step forward, Yellow Thearch disappeared from everyone's view, entering a dark room.

His forehead began to crack, from which an eyeball emerged. "Kill him!" a voice resounded from the eyeball. "Kill that brat!"

Its voice was full of fury.

The Element Spirit race had a deep foundation. Even Yellow Thearch couldn't tell how powerful the second civilization was.

In the face of everything in the Source World, the Element Spirit Civilization always seemed to remain calm.

But this time, it looked rather exasperated. "Kill whom?"

asked Yellow Thearch. "Zen!"

the eyeball nearly yelled back.

Even Emperor Charm had died because of Zen, so Yellow Thearch had figured he should pay attention to the man. Besides, the Descending Rings they had obtained couldn't be used successfully. He highly suspected that the golden red Chaotic Source Spirits in Zen's hand had something to do with it.

"Why the hurry?" asked Yellow Thearch.

"He has passed through the Soul City," the eyeball said.

"The Soul City? He's quite fast…" said Yellow Thearch plainly.

"He passed through the Soul City in a single try and obtained nine Holy Soul Imprints."

"What?"

At that, Yellow Thearch couldn't hide his shock.

The very idea of passing through the Soul City in a single try was truly astonishing.

What was even more bizarre was the fact that Zen could obtain nine Holy Soul Imprints—something that had never before happened on the Other Shore.

In fact, the news that Zen had obtained nine Holy Soul Imprints already spread through the Souls of Light in the Soul City.

But the internal structure of the Bearing race was complicated. It took some time for the news to spread layer by layer, delaying the dissemination. As a result, Yellow Thearch had yet to find out about what had happened to Dailey.

"Since he's already passed through the Soul City, I'm afraid he'll want to go to the Land of Bone Tribulation. We'd better snip him in the bud in Stage Thirty of the Other Shore," calculated Yellow Thearch.

He seemed to have a good understanding of Zen even without having met him personally.

Zen seemed to be the only special existence that entered the Other Shore.

He had his very own corporeal body.

When Yellow Thearch heard of the fact for the first time, he thought of the Eternal Scroll Painting—something Zen could possibly enter.

But at that time, Zen had just become famous in Stage Four of the Other Shore. There was a long way to go before he reached Stage Thirty-two of the Other Shore, so it wasn't the time to give it much mind.

In truth, he had even doubted that it was likely Zen could reach Stage Thirty-two alive.

But after only such a short time, Zen had already passed through the Soul City.

"Of course we will," continued the eyeball. "But for security's sake, you must take action in the Source World as well. You also need the golden red Chaotic Source Spirits, after all!"

'Must I personally lead the Bearing race?' Yellow Thearch wondered, narrowing his eyes.

Though Eastern Emperor Taiyi and Yasamin couldn't come back now, the Pear Hill wouldn't let them do anything easily. The fact made Yellow Thearch feel the need to set up certain strategies.

Meanwhile, on Stage Twenty-nine of the Other Shore… the Soul City had been open for one hundred and thirty-two hours, and it was time to close it.

Before the gate was shut, the Souls of Light in the Soul City emerged one after another.

From afar, Zen saw Elvinia step out wearing a grim expression. He, on the other hand, walked up to her with a smile and asked, "How is it going this time?"

"Eight hundred and ten feet," Elvinia answered with her head bowed. "I've tried my best, but I'm still too slow…"

"You're already very quick—you obviously already surpass Libby's talent in this aspect," Zen assured her.

But Elvinia merely pouted.

She didn't want the Soul City to become a restrictive barrier. She was very eager to pass through it.

This time, Elvinia had pushed herself to the limit. To a certain extent, even Libby, the top disciple of the Land of Sword Grief, couldn't catch up with her.

But so what? A great gap still remained between her and Zen. It was impossible for Zen to wait for her the entire time.

"The test in the Soul City is a form of training, so you shouldn't be anxious.

I'll wait for you in the Land of Bone Tribulation," Zen assured her.

Urgent was the current situation, so Zen had to press forward.

A Soul of Light nearby quickly walked over to them, carrying an aura that seemed far stronger than the ordinary. It was none other than Libby, who had already passed the test of the Soul City.

"Congratulations, Libby!"

"I didn't expect you to pass the test so soon!"

Both Gabriel and Carver were still around Libby.

Without Zen's incomprehensible record, Libby's performance was amazing in itself.

But over the past few days, all attention had been given to Zen, both inside and outside the Soul City.

Even Libby could feel that passing the test of the Soul City was a common thing—there was nothing to be excited about.

Once she arrived at Zen's side, she immediately said, "I've also passed the test of the Soul City. I want to go to Stage Thirty of the Other Shore and I heard that you know some kind of way to release the blood mist and dodge the Garudas. Can I go there with you?"

Libby hadn't had much interaction with Zen. When they first met, she had even provoked him. Now she felt rather bad having to ask him for help.

But Zen just smiled faintly and said, "We're both disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace, so we should help each other out on the Other Shore. If you need to go to a higher stage, I will help you, of course."

Zen's answer had Libby overjoyed with gratitude. "Thank you, Zen!"

It was quite normal for disciples in the Land of Sword Grief to communicate with each other with open arms, but for Elvinia, it was especially hard to accept. She secretly made up her mind about passing through the test of the Soul City as soon as she possibly could.

The Soul City was located at the very center of the Constant Glory Stage.

Behind it lay a long and narrow plank road.

At the end of it was a huge, round platform where densely distributed star rings led to the Blooming Jade Stage, Stage Thirty of the Other Shore.

Once he said goodbye to Elvinia, Zen used the Blood Fog Spell to cover both himself and Libby as they moved along the plank road. The moment they arrived at the huge round platform on the opposite end, Zen saw a Soul of Light of the Holy Soul Realm waiting for him.

The Soul of Light carried two wings on her back—she was a member of the Sun Crow race.

"Elizabeth?" Zen asked in a low voice.

While he couldn't quite see her face clearly, he was already well familiar with her aura after fighting against her several times.

Elizabeth's presence had Libby rather nervous until she remembered that the Sun Crow race no longer existed. The remaining members were dependent on Zen, so Libby could feel at ease.

Chapter 3739 Two Layers Under Zen's arrangement, all the members of the Sun Crow race had to stay in the Oneness Mountain for cultivation.

In reality, however, they were simply on standby.

The reason for that was if the Oneness Sky Palace ever encountered external intruders again, they would do their best to defend against them upon Zen's order.

Still, the only person those Sun Crows followed was the real Emperor Charm. After they knew about the current situation, they thought that they would never betray him.

Meanwhile, Elizabeth stared at Zen with an unreadable expression.

Both of them were at the Holy Soul Realm, but the aura Zen emitted was much stronger.

It made Elizabeth a little confused. "Zen, have you obtained the Holy Soul Imprint? How many did you get?" she asked.

For her, it was almost inevitable for Zen to obtain the Holy Soul Imprint.

However, she didn't know how many Holy Soul Imprints he could get.

Three or four? It might even be possible that he got five imprints.

While Elizabeth pondered over the matter, Libby, who was beside her, answered first, "Zen has passed through the Soul City on his first try and obtained nine Holy Soul Imprints."

Upon hearing those words, Elizabeth's Soul of Light suddenly trembled.

They even saw that the surface of her Soul of Light had fluctuated.

"Nine Holy Soul Imprints? Then, what did you see or what can you do with them?" she asked in a shaky voice.

Back then, she had gone to and returned from Stage Twenty-nine of the Other Shore so many times. Not even the Element Spirit race could unravel the secret about the Soul City.

If Zen obtained nine Holy Soul Imprints, then he might have obtained different opportunities.

"He can open and close the door of the Soul City freely," Libby said.

On the other hand, Zen glanced at Libby. He was slightly thankful that she answered the questions for him.

Now, Elizabeth asked such questions just out of curiosity.

However, he refused to reveal the secret of the Starry Roc-fish in the Soul City.

"Yes." He nodded, and then continued, "There is a switch to the door on top of the Soul City."

Only then did Elizabeth realize that she had asked something she shouldn't have asked.

If she talked to another master or even Emperor Charm that way, she might get punished.

Yet, Zen had only avoided the topic.

As soon as she came back to her senses, she changed the subject and said, "Zen, you should stay in the Constant Glory Stage for now.

Don't go to the Blooming Jade Stage." "Why?" Zen asked curiously.

"If you go there, the Element Spirit race would attack you. They would never let you set foot in the Land of Bone Tribulation," Elizabeth replied.

Since she had followed Emperor Charm while traveling on the Other Shore, she had witnessed how strong the Element Spirit Civilization was.

In her opinion, it was almost impossible for anyone to defeat the unbeatable Element Spirit Civilization.

"Just because they will attack me in the Blooming Jade Stage like you said, I have to stay in the Constant Glory Stage all my life?" asked Zen.

Elizabeth was stunned at Zen's question.

"Some paths are destined to be difficult, but we can't stop because of some obstacles," he said indifferently.

In turn, Elizabeth was silent for a moment. However, she had already expected such an answer from him.

"If you want to go, please follow me. I'm very familiar with both the Blooming Jade Stage and the Element Spirit race. Although it's a bit risky, I can help you reach Stage Thirty-one of the Other Shore!" she offered.

Libby blinked and said, "The masters of our Oneness Sky Palace will be there to meet us. He doesn't need you."

Although she knew that Elizabeth had already surrendered and wouldn't attack Zen, there was still a chance that she might do so.

Elizabeth glanced at Libby, and then at Zen. Zen was the one to make the decision.

"I want to get there with my physical body, not my Soul of Light. I'll be back after I change my form. If you have better way to pass through the Blooming Jade Stage, then of course I will choose the easier way," Zen said with a nod.

After all, his top priority right now was to go to the Land of Bone Tribulation. He didn't want to stay in Stage Thirty of the Other Shore.

If his Soul of Light ever went there in the future, then there would probably be a fierce battle between him and the Element Spirit race.

"Then I'll wait for you here," Elizabeth agreed with a smile.

After they were done, Zen left the Other Shore with his Soul of Light and entered it again with his physical body. He continued to use the Blood Fog Spell to move forward.

When he arrived at the star ring, Elizabeth and Libby were still waiting for him.

"Libby, I'm afraid I'll be in trouble when I go to the Blooming Jade Stage this time. Why don't you stay here and wait for a while before going there?"

he suggested.

Libby just chuckled at him and said, "Well, I have also stepped into the Holy Soul Realm , so my Soul of Light isn't as fragile as an ordinary Soul of Light."

"You do indeed have the strength to fight against a physical body after you've reached the Holy Soul Realm, but it is vastly different when you are against a truly powerful Other Shore creature. There is still a big difference between your strength and theirs. I suggest you stay here for the time being," Elizabeth said coldly.

When she talked to Libby, she became as arrogant as she was before.

Libby slowly answered, "Thank you for your concern, but I don't need anyone to give me any advice."

"Let's go!" Zen declared.

He did not want to participate in such a meaningless argument, so he walked straight to the star ring.

In just a second, Elizabeth and Libby stepped into the star ring as well and turned into white beams of light that shot upwards.

From Stage Twenty-nine of the Other Shore, almost every stage had a specific arrangement.

Stage Twenty-nine of the Other Shore had the Soul City, Stage Thirty-one had the Land of Bone Tribulation, and Stage Thirty-two housed the Eternal Scroll Painting.

Only Stage Thirty of the Other Shore was considered normal! Therefore, the disputes in Stage Thirty had been the most intense since many chaotic eras ago. It was even safe to say that most races would fight for Stage Thirty.

But since the human race was trapped in Stage Thirty-three of the Other Shore and the Nihility race was always on the defensive, the Element Spirit Civilization gradually took control of Stage Thirty. A large number of the members from the Element Spirit race stayed in Stage Thirty, which they considered as their headquarters.

"Swoosh..."

The moment Zen left the star ring, the turbulent cold air blew over his body and made him stiff.

When Libby walked out of the star ring, she also felt that her Soul of Light was about to solidify.

She would've gotten injured if it wasn't for her Colorless Soul.

As for Elizabeth, she had already adapted to the low temperature in the Blooming Jade Stage, so she was well prepared.

"What a vast ice field!" Zen exclaimed as he looked into the distance.

The ice field was boundless, and it seemed that the entire Blooming Jade Stage was made of ice. There were even rays of icy light that shone down from the sky above the Blooming Jade Stage.

Zen stared at the sky for a while and asked, "Is there another layer of ice above the Blooming Jade Stage?"

He looked around carefully and found that the ice light above them did not refract from below. It looked like there was another layer of ice above their heads.

"Yes, there are two layers on the Blooming Jade Stage. The upper layer is extremely cold and could freeze both Other Shore creatures and the Souls of Light.

No one can cross the upper layer, so we can only pass through the lower layer of ice," Libby explained.

In other words, all the living beings in the entire Blooming Jade Stage and the many temples and strongholds of various forces were all sandwiched between the two layers of ice. "I wonder what better way of passing through you have come up with, Elizabeth," Libby said and glanced at Elizabeth.

A faint smile graced Elizabeth's lips, and she said, "The better way I mentioned is to pass through the upper ice field."

Chapter 3740 Penetrating Through The Ice Libby was stunned for a while when she heard Elizabeth's suggestion. Then, she said, "What? Did you just suggest that we go through the upper ice field? Are you trying to kill us?"

The upper ice field was a forbidden area in the Blooming Jade Stage! If there wasn't a lower ice field, perhaps no one would've made their way to Stage Thirty-one.

"Well, I have to admit that I am only interested in Zen's life. As for yours… I'm not interested in the slightest. You don't have to come with me if you don't want!" Elizabeth retorted.

At that moment, Zen chimed in and asked, "But since the upper ice field is so dangerous, why did you choose that path?"

"According to your current situation, it's almost impossible for you to go through Stage Thirty in the normal way, unless you can overturn the entire Element Spirit Civilization with your strength," Elizabeth explained.

Elizabeth had always analyzed things from a third-person point of view.

For instance, she was well aware of both Zen's ability and the strength of the Element Spirit Civilization.

Now, the death of Emperor Charm wasn't a big loss for the Element Spirit Civilization, but they might have paid greater attention to Zen.

What was worse was that the news Zen had passed through the Soul City might have caused a stir.

Based on the current situation, he knew that the powerful warriors of the Sun Crow race had no choice but to follow him. Furthermore, she could never deceive him due to the influence of the bloodline worship.

Now that Zen had agreed, Elizabeth decided to stop arguing with Libby.

With a gentle flick of her wings, she flew up into the air and said, "I know of a way that leads to the upper ice field. Follow me!"

When Zen was about to activate the Thunder Materialization, he suddenly looked at Libby. An ordinary Soul of Light couldn't fly, but he still didn't know if a Holy Soul, which was also named Colorless Soul, was able to.

To his surprise, several lines appeared on Libby's back and glowed brightly, then she quickly floated upwards and rose into the air.

'So a Holy Soul could fly…' he thought as a pair of thunder wings formed behind his back.

The crack of thunder filled the air, then he also flew up and followed closely behind Elizabeth.

As they flew in the sky, they saw that the distance between the lower and upper ice fields was over a hundred thousand feet! Therefore, it was no easy feat to fly from the lower ice field to the upper one.

At the same time, the temperature of the air around them became lower and lower as they continued to fly higher.

"Swoosh!"

A strong gust of numbingly cold wind blew over their faces.

If such powerful winds caught even an ultimate-level Indigo Soul, then they would freeze to death and shatter into pieces.

When the winds blew over Elizabeth, the meridians in her soul glowed and she easily resisted the cold.

Meanwhile, Libby had much more difficulty doing so since she had just reached the Holy Soul Realm. When she saw how Elizabeth dealt with the cold, she followed suit and the meridians in her soul also started to flicker with light. She managed to expel all the cold air that invaded her Colorless Soul in this way.

As for Zen...

Although he did feel cold, he could still withstand it and didn't even bother to put up any defenses.

After the three of them reached a height of one hundred thousand feet, they finally arrived beneath the upper ice field.

Zen reached out his hand and touched the thick ice sheet above him. The moment his fingers touched it, white frost quickly spread around his hand like a monster's tentacles.

He tried to pull his hand out, only to find that it was stuck firmly to the ice! Just as he was about to summon his strength to forcefully withdraw his hand, a ball of golden flames burst from the side and burned his hand.

Phew! The flames blazed in his hand and quickly melted the white frost, and thus freed him from the ice.

"Be careful not to touch the ice," Elizabeth warned.

Zen smiled with embarrassment and silently followed her.

However, that sort of danger wasn't actually a problem for him. In fact, he could break through the thick ice directly if he wanted to — but on second thought, he remembered that their goal was to pass through the Blooming Jade Stage without being noticed.

Therefore, he decided not to mess things around and just follow Elizabeth's instructions.

They flew along the ice sheet for a long while until they seemed to have arrived at the very edge of the Blooming Jade Stage.

There was a shallow channel at the edge of the ice sheet. Elizabeth flew straight into the channel, then her body began to emit the divine flame of the Sun Crow race.

There were a few sizzling sounds, then thick, white fog spread out from where the fire and ice combined.

After Zen and Libby watched Elizabeth melt the ice for a while, the two of them heard her voice from above that said, "The ice sheet is about a thousand feet thick. Follow me, or you will get frozen in the ice."

In turn, Zen and Libby went into the hole Elizabeth created and followed her into the ice.

Like several moths that bore through a thick book, they slowly penetrated through the ice sheet with the help of the divine flames.

Soon enough, Elizabeth was worn out from keeping the divine flames active for a long time.

After she had advanced over two hundred feet in the ice, she stopped to rest. "May I try?" Zen suddenly offered.

Elizabeth looked at Zen in surprise. "Can you use a fire of the same level?"

she asked.

The flames created from Godly Ways couldn't melt the ice at this place.

After all, they were in the Blooming Jade Stage, Stage Thirty of the Other Shore! Any block of ice in the area was an Other Shore Token with ice attributes.

"I can't, but someone else can!"

He communicated with the Primeval Lord of Heaven in his mind, then gently waved his hand. A fire lotus bloomed in his palm.

Whoosh! The fire lotus rotated gracefully as it flew towards the ice above.

Hissss! It was Zhurong, the God of Fire, who had summoned the fire lotus.

Even if he was only an energy soul of the real Zhurong, the fire lotus still possessed compelling powers.

The ice melted quickly under the fire lotus' flames, and clouds of white mist immediately enveloped the three of them.

"The ice melts so fast!" Elizabeth exclaimed as she looked at the rising fire lotus with astonishment.

The fire lotus created a cave that was more than two hundred feet long, before it gradually went out.

"Let's go!" Zen shouted.

"Go!"

When Zen reached the end of the cave, he summoned another fire lotus in his palm.

Zzzztttt...

In the next second, a strange and shrill sound came from above.

The fire lotus had penetrated the ice sheet, then strong gales of cold wind howled from above.

The cold winds were quite powerful. It caught Zen, Elizabeth, and Libby off guard as they dropped a certain distance. It was like a huge, invisible hand had slapped them.

Among them, Zen dropped the shortest length, followed by Elizabeth, while Libby dropped the most.

Fortunately, the cold winds only raged for three seconds before the broken ice sheet froze again. After the opening was blocked, the cold winds were gone.

"Such strong winds…The upper ice field is truly worthy of its reputation,"

Zen remarked with a smile.

He was fully covered in white frost, and so were Elizabeth and Libby.

Chapter 3741 Cold Prisons Libby couldn't help but sigh dejectedly. "If it's already awfully cold at the entrance, how much colder will it be above? I can't imagine what that'll be like," she said while shivering slightly.

However, Elizabeth merely shrugged indifferently. "To be honest, this is not the coldest place yet. You will know when you get up there!"

Obviously, Emperor Charm had obtained a great deal of benefits from the Element Spirit race when he joined them.

Elizabeth began floating towards Zen. As soon as she passed by him, she had released the divine flames of the Sun Crow race on her fingertips.

The temperature of the Divine Fire Shield itself was not that high. However, it was able to control the temperature within a certain range.

Elizabeth said.

"Bang!"

Under the protection of the Divine Fire Shield, the three of them dashed upward together.

They broke through the ice-cold hole that was now starting to freeze over.

After a while, the trio finally arrived at the upper ice field. They made it with almost no problem at all.

Whoosh! Whoosh... Suddenly they heard a loud swishing sound.

They encountered a fierce cold wind that blew over them. It was quite powerful and should not be taken lightly. It almost overturned the Divine Fire Shield.

"Hold on!" Elizabeth's facial expression changed.

If the Divine Fire Shield was blown away by this monstrous wind, their fate would be sealed. They could already imagine getting frozen to death in this icy wasteland.

Without second thought, Zen immediately clasped the Divine Fire Shield in his hands with lightning speed. He gripped it as tightly as he could. No matter how hard the cold wind blew, the Divine Fire Shield did not budge at all. It remained covering the three of them! Elizabeth breathed a sigh of relief. If Zen hadn't reacted quickly, the shield would have overturned. "Let's keep moving forward!" She motioned them to follow her. "Over there on the left, you can see the line that marks the end of the ice field. As long as we continue to walk along the line, we should be on the right way... "

The area of Blooming Jade Stage was quite immense.

Even though the path Elizabeth had chosen was considered relatively safe, it still was not that easy to cross.

The only thing they encountered in the boundless ice field was the cold bitter wind that blew hard. Other than the vast blue and white ice field, they couldn't see anything else. Not even a single snowflake was in sight.

Every five minutes, the red light on the Divine Fire Shield would start to dim. In addition to that, the temperature under the shield would also plummet. Every time this would happen, Elizabeth would send a divine flame toward the Divine Fire Shield with just a slight flick of her finger.

The light of the Divine Fire Shield would once again become bright.

A few hours had already passed since the three of them had made their way above the ice field. However, all they could see in front of them was just pure white space. They couldn't see the way in front of them or the way they had passed.

"We can't just keep going on like this. It's too slow and we're wasting too much time already," Zen said impatiently. "Can't we just fly over?"

He asked because he knew Elizabeth was able to fly. However, she merely shook her head when she heard Zen's suggestion. "The situation on the ice field is completely different from what you actually see. There are some extremely cold and turbulent currents up in the air that are invisible. If we ever get caught up in those currents, even the Divine Fire Shield won't be able to protect us."

All he could do now was to keep moving forward under the shield.

After they had walked for another sixteen hours, the cold wind gradually stopped.

Without the sound of the wind, the place was so quiet. It was such a deafening silence.

"The cold wind has stopped blowing?" Zen noticed this immediately. He looked around him through the shield. He couldn't feel the wind anymore.

Elizabeth merely shrugged. "Well, that's because the temperature is much lower here than where we were before."

It was common knowledge that as the temperature reached an extremely low point, any kind of energy would become almost stagnant. The cold wind on the ice field was also considered as a powerful energy.

"Hey, Zen! Look! What's that over there?" Libby had been quietly observing the area around them all along.

She already knew that it would be very cold on the Blooming Jade Stage.

However, never in her dreams did she think that the upper ice field would be like this.

Northwest of their current location, they saw a portion of the ice field sinking for a few dozen feet. It seemed like there was nothing in that area at all. However, they felt that this zone exuded a particularly huge pressure.

Zen stared at the area that Libby pointed out. Then, his facial expression was filled with utter curiosity. Instinctively, he grabbed the Divine Fire Shield and tried to move towards that area.

"No, wait! Don't go there!"

Elizabeth hurriedly pulled the Divine Fire Shield. She said, "That's a Cold Prison. Don't go there!"

Elizabeth nodded. "The temperature in there is much lower than that of where we are standing right now. That makes it the third coldest place on the entire Other Shore." She began discharging a divine flame of the Sun Crow race upon her fingertips and turned it into a small flame arrow. She shot the flame arrow made of incredibly condensed heat towards the Cold Prison.

Whoosh! It soared directly towards the Cold Prison.

Strangely enough, the flame arrow suddenly stopped the moment it entered the Cold Prison.

The arrow seemed like it was hovering steadily and slowly. Even the flame on it was flickering very slowly as well.

"The flame arrow looks oddly peculiar," mumbled Zen as he stared at the arrow.

He thought that if the "Cold Prison" was truly extremely cold, then the flame arrow should have been extinguished right away.

In this case, the flame didn't go out immediately. Instead, it actually looked like it was burning really slowly.

"Believe it or not, the flame arrow has already been extinguished,"

explained Elizabeth. "But due to the extremely low temperature of the Cold Prison, time has been oddly distorted inside. The flame arrow that you see floating slowly right now is merely a mirage."

Whenever something had reached an extreme level, it was usually enough to render some parts of the basic rules ineffective.

As the coldness reached its absolute limit, the properties of many things would also change.

"Sizzle!"

After the flame arrow floated for a few seconds, it suddenly burned brightly.

In a split second, the entire Cold Prison was filled with firelight.

Nevertheless, the firelight just flashed quickly and disappeared without a trace.

The moment the firelight illuminated the Cold Prison, Zen noticed some light dots with strange shapes that appeared inside it. Those light dots were randomly distributed and they looked very similar to the light dots in the Abstruse Energy World.

"So those light dots are..."

Just as Zen was about to ask, Elizabeth began to explain. "So far, we still don't know what those light dots are. But I have heard from Emperor Charm that there are some things imprisoned here. That is why these areas on the ice field are called 'Cold Prisons'."

Simply put, the Cold Prisons on Stage Thirty actually imprisoned the creatures from the Abstruse Energy World.

It was too bad that Geoffrey had been left in the Deleting Space. If he was here, Zen would be able to ask him to tell what these light dots were.

Driven by his absolute curiosity, Zen also flicked a few flames towards the Cold Prison. He observed them carefully just as he did earlier.

As soon as the flames entered the Cold Prison, they all floated slowly like Elizabeth's flame arrow. Then with a flash of firelight, they disappeared too.

After trying several more times, Zen continued to move forward under the Divine Fire Shield.

Soon enough, he discovered that there were Cold Prisons everywhere on the upper ice field.

The densely packed Cold Prisons looked like they were holes that had been dug by worms. They had cut the originally sleek ice surface into many parts.

Chapter 3742 The Core Of The Heavenly Obsession Civilization They had to step carefully since, according to Elizabeth, the Cold Prisons were horrible and dangerous.

Fortunately, the prisons were special. The temperature inside was indeed extremely low, but it would not hurt them even if they got very close.

"Did you say that the Cold Prisons are not the coldest, but the third coldest?" Zen asked questioning how that could be true.

From what he had seen just now, it seemed the temperature inside was already low to the extreme. Under such a temperature, even time and space had undergone a qualitative change; he found it hard to imagine an environment that could be colder than that.

"You will soon see the second coldest place," said Elizabeth. "But the place with the lowest temperature on the Other Shore is said to be on Stage Thirty-three. I have only heard of it, never seen it."

"I'll soon see the second coldest place..."

Zen repeated to himself, trying to restrain his curiosity. He walked slowly on the path between the Cold Prisons, under the protection of the Divine Fire Shield.

"In a Cold Prison, it would take almost all the water in a sea to create a thumb-sized ice cube. Look over there..."

Not far away, on the left, was a very special looking Cold Prison. The others were empty, but this Cold Prison held a small ice cube the size of a thumb in the center...

Zen's jaw dropped slightly as he thought of what Elizabeth had just said.

Within the Bright Sea Province was an island and a city, and the rest was all sea.

"It would take an enormous amount of water to condense it to surround this metal box. How could there be so much water in this world?" Zen asked utterly astounded and dumbfounded.

Elizabeth smiled and revealed, "That mystery is still unsolved. Or at least the Element Spirit race could not solve it."

The Other Shore had many similar mysteries and secrets spread throughout.

The Element Spirit Civilization had been active on the Other Shore for more than one thousand chaotic eras, yet they still hadn't been able to figure it out.

Zen nodded and moved around the metal box under the shield.

He had felt a sense of familiarity when he first saw this metal box. Its shape was very similar to that of the Civilization Artifact of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization.

But the shape was quite simple and common, so it wasn't strange that they looked alike. He decided not to say anything in the end.

But then, just as Zen and the others walked from behind the metal box to the front, the Primeval Lord of Heaven's voice suddenly rang out. "Zen, the Civilization Artifact of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization has issued a task again."

Zen was slightly stunned to hear this.

The Heavenly Obsession Civilization had been issuing tasks tirelessly, but Zen was not interested in receiving any of them and thus ignored them.

However, ever since the Primeval Lord of Heaven had entered his inner world, a person had been sent specifically to guard the Civilization Artifact.

This person classified and recorded every task issued by the Civilization Artifact.

The recorder was never tired of the work, recording all tasks and classifying them according to different levels; heaven-level, earth-level, first-class, second-class and so on. He recorded everything, not missing a word, and then meticulously reported them to the Primeval Lord of Heaven.

Today, the Heavenly Obsession Civilization had suddenly issued a task.

"Special task: return to the core of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization! Reward: nothing!"

This strange task stunned the recorder.

The tasks issued were never the same. The level and class of the tasks, as well as the reward that would be offered for completing them, would be announced clearly.

Now, the Civilization Aircraft suddenly issued such an unusual task, which baffled the recorder.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven had also warned him that he should report anything unusual to him immediately. This was one of those cases and so the recorder hurriedly reported it to the Primeval Lord of Heaven, who then promptly brought it to Zen's attention.

"Special task...

Return to the core of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization..."

Zen's face twisted strangely at what he had just learned.

If this was what was now put before him, then the Heavenly Obsession Civilization must have something to do with this huge metal box. Was this the core of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization? Finally, Zen, Elizabeth and Libby made it to the front of the box.

Just then, something began to change.

A speck of red light flickered dimly on the metal box...

It spread from the bottom to the top of the metal box, which then began trembling vaguely.

"What's happening?"

This switched Elizabeth's expression dramatically.

This huge metal box had stood on the upper ice field for countless years.

No one had even gotten close to it, let alone seen it move.

The sudden change had startled her.

"Crack!"

The ice on the surface of the metal box cracked.

If a thumb-sized ice cube would require the water of a sea to be condensed into it, one could only imagine the kind of power needed to break such thick ice.

"Retreat! Hurry!"

An ice block the size of a fist fell from above and crashed into the ice field.

"Crack!"

This highly condensed ice block held an amount of water equivalent to a huge sea the size of several provinces.

The upper ice field was unable to support it at all. The ice block smashed right into it, penetrating the thick layer of ice, and smashing into the lower ice field.

Luckily, this area on the lower ice field was unpopulated. The ice block had not fallen on any living creatures. The only damage caused was a small pit in the ground, left by the ice block before it disappeared without a trace...

Many more ice blocks fell similarly.

To be safe, Zen, Elizabeth and Libby had all retreated. A long while later, most of the blocks of ice at the front of the metal box had fallen off.

A dark red light silently began glowing to reveal the outline of a door.

"It has a door. Does that mean we can go inside?" Elizabeth was overtaken by excitement.

She had passed by here many times and had always regarded this place as forbidden and not to be approached. Anyone who witnessed this sudden change would be as excited as she now was.

Chapter 3743 Two Civilizations Elizabeth had always been careful ever since she set foot on the upper ice field, but now she was finally feeling a little bit radical.

"Come on! Let's go over there and have a look!" she excitedly said to the other two.

At this moment, however, Zen became extremely cautious and wary. "Wait a moment. There are still some ice blocks that haven't fallen off. It's not a joke when you get hit by these ice blocks."

As soon as he finished speaking, another large chunk of hard transparent ice fell from above. With a clash, it created a massive hole in the ice field.

The three of them waited at a distance for some more time. They didn't continue their slow approach until there was a clear sign that there would no longer be any solid ice falling.

The door outlined by the light was still closed like before.

Fearing that the metal box would be too cold to touch, Elizabeth immediately released a divine flame of the Sun Crow race.

The divine flame was burning the surface of the metal box, but it did not extinguish quickly. It was like any ordinary flame, burning for a while before it quietly dwindled.

"There is no problem with the metal box, but how can we get in?" Elizabeth asked as she shook her head.

Zen and Elizabeth shifted their eyes to the center of the door at the same time. It was not until Libby pointed out that they noticed that the center of the black metal door was indeed sunken.

"I wonder, what can be put in this sunken area?" Elizabeth asked. She looked really confused.

However, Zen's heart skipped a beat at that same moment.

Judging from the size and shape of the sunken area, it was completely the same with the size and shape of the Civilization Artifact of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization. It seemed that the movement of this huge metal box had something to do with the Civilization Artifact under his control.

"I think I may know," Zen said with a smirk.

Elizabeth and Libby curiously looked at Zen at the same time. Of course, the two girls hadn't imagined that all of this had been caused by Zen.

"Buzz..."

It was still a little troublesome to take out an Other Shore Token that had already been carried before.

"This box..."

"It seems to be just the right size!"

Libby's and Elizabeth's eyes abruptly lit up with excitement.

Zen pushed the Civilization Artifact into the sunken area. The Civilization Artifact perfectly fitted and matched with the sunken area.

"Buzz!"

"It's open..."

Elizabeth said in disbelief.

Things went on almost unimaginably smoothly.

It was as if the path of the upper ice field was made specifically for Zen.

After absorbing the Civilization Artifact into his inner world, Zen was cautious enough to not rush into the metal box immediately. Like Elizabeth, he released a fire column first to test the temperature inside the metal box.

After the fire column went inside, the temperature did not change that much. Only then did Zen enter with the shield for caution.

Rays of green light could be seen, which made the inside of the metal box look like there were little snakes wandering along the wall.

Elizabeth shook her head as if she was saying that she didn't know the answer to Libby's question. She had also never encountered a thing like this before.

"You have completed the task of entering the core of Heavenly Obsession Civilization, and your reward for this is the activation of the core of Heavenly Obsession Civilization."

When the Civilization Artifact made this sound, the number of rays of green light on the wall greatly increased. As thousands of rays of green light flowed on the wall, the entire metal box was immediately reflecting in an eerie green glow.

Elizabeth and Libby warily looked around as they squeezed beside Zen with nervous expressions on their faces. If there was a trap, then they would all be doomed.

Not to mention other things but even if a Cold Prison covered them, they would all be frozen to their core.

Being squeezed by the two girls, Zen was at a loss for words. He could only say, "It's me who activated the light."

Zen just shook his head and said, "I haven't figured out that part either."

Just as the two of them were discussing, a ray of light suddenly shot out from a wall right in front of them.

The light swept across Elizabeth, Zen, and Libby. Then a green shadow slowly appeared on the wall in front of them. Judging from the curvaceous silhouette, it should be a shadow of a human woman. Its size and form were actually remarkably similar to that of Elizabeth.

When Zen looked at the green figure from head to toe, it suddenly spoke in a tuneful voice.

"Hello..."

This voice was incredibly special. It was neither a voice of a woman nor a man, neither a voice of a child nor an elder. It sounded as if there were multiple people—males and females, young and old—speaking at the same time. Judging by the sound ray alone, it was terribly like the Civilization Artifact of the Heavenly Obsession Civilization.

With the theurgies on the Other Shore, all sorts of things could be created.

However, a consciousness could never be created.

Just like what Zen thought, he also thought that the green figure was a soul fragment.

"No, I am not a soul fragment. I am not attached to anyone. I am an independent individual and I was created," the green figure replied affirmatively. Obviously, it understood what a soul fragment was, but it didn't think it was a soul fragment.

The light that formed the green figure flickered and then suddenly disappeared.

All kinds of illusions and magic arrays in chaos were very ordinary theurgies.

"The means may seem very difficult for you to do, but it's extremely simple for us," the green figure said.

"The Heavenly Obsession Civilization was actually the second chaotic era we have experienced. The experiences in that round of chaos have been annihilated in history. Chapter 3744 The Civilization Made Up Of Insects Zen had long since heard of the Calculation Civilization.

They were the ones who advocated for another way to complete the Finale Way.

Instead of relying on the Other Shore, the Calculation Civilization completely abandoned that strategy and used their own understanding of space, time, and energy to carry out the Finale Way.

It was said that they almost succeeded but that claim was never confirmed since very little trace of their culture and history remained, which was why not a lot of civilizations believed they were able to almost complete the Finale Way.

Despite that, however, the Primeval Lord of Heaven still acutely learned this. He put the information about the Energy Shaft into the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Tree.

The Pear Hill finally chose to let Yan cultivate the Energy Shaft. In the Chaotic Source World, she had used it once.

However, it was worth noting that the Energy Shaft she wielded was only rudimentary. The real Energy Shaft could alter time, space, and energy freely. Its power was unimaginably great.

Libby had never heard of the Calculation Civilization or the Heavenly Obsession Civilization before. Elizabeth knew a bit about them but never really thought highly of them. It was the Primeval Lord of Heaven who made Zen ask the question.

In order to sow the seeds of the human race, the Primeval Lord of Heaven paid a heavy price and it was only by taking advantage of the opportunity when the chaotic era moved onto the next one was he able to succeed.

For the Heavenly Obsession Civilization to have served as a ruling civilization in two chaotic eras was unheard of! "Because we discovered the method of passing down our civilization," the green being answered.

"Our civilization is different from other civilizations," the green figure continued. "These are our real forms."

It was very common for insects to form civilizations.

"In our Calculation Civilization, male members release red light while female members release green..."

Dots of red and green light paired up with each other. As the insects bonded, red and green light began to flash constantly.

It wasn't just him. Both Elizabeth and Libby were equally, if not more, confused.

"This is a calculation method," the green figure answered. "You humans have ten fingers and calculate with the decimal system but for us, we count by two colors, red and green, with the binary system..."

This talk about counting methods confused Zen but the Primeval Lord of Heaven appeared above him and directly asked his question. "What is the advantage of this binary system?"

"Advantage?" the green figure repeated. "The advantage is that we have unparalleled calculation ability."

With this revelation, the scene before them began to change.

Tens of thousands, millions, hundreds of millions...

Red and green lined up together and flickered continuously. As the insects gathered together, they calculated the results and communicated with each other.

"Such a special method of calculation!" the Primeval Lord of Heaven exclaimed with excitement. "Just how powerful is it?"

"It can easily decipher Sanskrit words," the green figure replied.

When the Primeval Lord of Heaven heard this, his expression changed.

For so many years, Geoffrey was the only one he knew who was able to decipher Sanskrit words with his inborn ability. The boy was just able to understand the words naturally! The Calculation Civilization's method was completely different. They deciphered Sanskrit words through terrifying calculation! As a result, the Sanskrit words, which might be secrets to others, were nothing mysterious to them.

It was through their faultless calculation method that the civilization was able to decipher all Sanskrit words and evolved at such a fast pace.

"If that's the case then why does nobody know of your civilization?" the Primeval Lord of Heaven asked.

He had a point. Such an advanced ruling civilization would've definitely left marks on the Other Shore, not unverifiable rumors.

Zen couldn't help but nod in agreement.

"Ha-ha..."

To their surprise, the green figure laughed. "We're too small, even smaller than the tiniest mosquito in your world. It's difficult for individuals in our civilization to increase their strength all alone."

It was indeed true. The insects were incredibly small, just like the indecipherable grains of sand on a beach.

A civilization of micro-individuals would have trouble producing powerful existences.

"Don't be mistaken though. Even if we are small, we still have the means to cultivate. An individual's strength may not be that impressive, but together..."

Countless insects began to appear and flash a barrage of lights on the wall.

These insects combined in a special way to form an indomitable force that could fight against ferocious beasts in that chaotic era.

Alone, they were weak, but together, they could be unstoppable. Thus, the Calculation Civilization cultivated as a unit.

This was the same method No. 9527 adopted inside the Chaos Ancient God Gerald's mind. Each soul fragment had a mind of its own but combined, they formed a complete whole.

Chapter 3745 The Remarkable Calculation Ability An expression of surprise flashed across the Primeval Lord of Heaven's face, "You have already made it?"

Chapter 3746 The Failure Of The Heavenly Obsession Civilization According to the Calculation Civilization's assumption, the Energy Shaft's transformation ability was virtually infinite.
