The Ear Mice stopped running and breathed a collective sigh of relief when the Ghost-claw Worms were finally killed.

"We got rid of them!"

"Zen, we would have died if it weren't for you!"

"What a coincidence! You saved my son in the Chaotic Source World before. You hadn't stepped into the Desire World at the time. I haven't expected you to reach the Sanskrit Light Stage and save my life," one of the Ear Mice exclaimed.

The three Ear Mice were expressing their gratitude when Libby suddenly asked, "But where are we now?"

At her question, the Ear Mice began to panic. Caught up in the chase that the Ghost-claw Worms had given them, they had no idea which bone cave they were in now.

Chapter 3768 Outside Libby's question made Zen and the three Ear Mice realize this was a problem that needed to be addressed.

The bone caves in the Sanskrit Light Stage formed the most complicated maze any of them had ever come across. Up until now, there was still no one who had completely worked out the entire maze.

"Deviating too far from our original route would be disastrous, I'm afraid,"

Fidel said seriously.

Zen considered their options for a while before finally saying, "Those Ghost-claw Worms always leave traces, and we can go back the same way we came by following those traces they've left."

After that, he turned and began walking back.

Zen had sliced the Ghost-claw Worms' heads off at the neck and they still struggled on the ground. Even now they still stretched out three fingers in an attempt to grab Zen as he passed.

"Whoosh!"

The long sword in Zen's hand shook, and with a flash of sword radiance, he had cut the wriggling heads in halves.

Zen and the Ear Mice felt more comfortable with their plan after seeing these Ghost-claw Worms. Zen had killed many along the way so it'd be an easy trail to follow back...

They followed the corpses, walking the wrong way on several occasions before they had finally found the original path they had taken here.

The Ear Mice had come from a different bone cave and recorded a different path. Now they too, like Zen, were counting on Libby to lead the way.

Fortunately, although it was Libby's first time in the Sanskrit Light Stage, she was very smart and remembered the way to the Land of Bone Tribulation clearly.

"There are eight bone caves in the bone cavity. We should take the seventh one..."

"There are two roads here. We should take the left one..."

"The first bone cave..."

Under her guidance, they continued onward, slightly uphill.

Just as Fidel had said, they were in fact still in the sea formed by the Soul Interdicting Water. If they broke through a wall of a bone cave, the Soul Interdicting Water would gush in.

But many bones were in the water, looking like countless tubes.

The route the Ear Mice had taken had been submerged by the Soul Interdicting Water, but everything was fine for the one the human race had recorded in their documents, and they continued smoothly along the way.

The size of the Sanskrit Light Stage was no smaller than that of the Blooming Jade Stage. Zen and his companions climbed up the bone caves for four hours before they finally came to a huge bone cavity.

There were many bone caves of different sizes here. The largest was massive and the smallest was only as big as a fist.

Zen looked around and said, "It seems that all the bone caves are connected to this bone cavity?"

"Yes, this one is our Ear Mice's bone cave," said Fidel, pointing at a cave that was neither too big nor too small. "That is the bone cave of the Separate Abyss race... Eh?"

Fidel shrieked as it pointed at a wide bone cave. It was so large that even those of the Separate Abyss race could walk through it freely. This was indeed their bone cave. But there was something odd about it; a green light flashed at the entrance of the cave as if reflected by a mirror. It soon discovered that the entire cave had been filled with Soul Interdicting Water! "What's wrong?"

Zen and Libby had noticed Fidel's strange reaction immediately. They walked over to have a closer look and were both shocked at what they saw.

"Whose bone cave is this?" Zen asked.

"The Separate Abyss race!" exclaimed Fidel.

"It seems that the Separate Abyss race have it much worse. Their cave is filled with the Soul Interdicting Water. I wonder if there's anyone trapped within it," Zen mused, shaking his head.

As Zen climbed higher up the stages of the Other Shore, the number of Souls of Light he could meet lowered. There was only the Land of Bone Tribulation on the huge Sanskrit Light Stage where warriors could explore.

A warrior like Libby, who had reached the Holy Soul Realm, would usually choose to pass through the Sanskrit Light Stage and go directly to Stage Thirty-two, the destination of the powerful Holy Souls.

"Splash..."

As they looked on, the Soul Interdicting Water had risen by a foot! When it eventually overflowed it would probably pour into the other bone caves around it.

"Let's go! The bone cave is full of Soul Interdicting Water. Who knows what monsters might burst from it," Libby urged standing aside.

Zen nodded in agreement and looked up at the other end of the bone cavity.

"I wonder which bone cave leads to the Land of Bone Tribulation..."

There were many bone caves of various sizes around the huge cavity, but in the center were three bone caves that extended up diagonally. It was Zen's first time here but he understood enough to know that the exit of the Sanskrit Light Stage was among these three caves.

"Zen, Are you heading to the Land of Bone Tribulation?" Fidel asked excitedly.

Since ancient times, no one in the chaos had been able to enter the Land of Bone Tribulation.

Over the years, only a small number of Other Shore creatures had gone there, but no one in the chaos had the necessary qualifications to enter.

"Yes." Zen nodded.

"We'll be taking the cave in the middle to go to Stage Thirty-two. To get to the Land of Bone Tribulation, you should go through the cave on the left."

Fidel said enviously, "If you succeed, you'll be the first to qualify to enter the Eternal Scroll Painting after ancient times!"

This was important news to the Ear Mice and when Fidel could leave the Other Shore, it would surely bring it to the superiors immediately.

Libby looked at Zen in silence. She knew the left bone cave led to the Land of Bone Tribulation, but because she couldn't go there herself, she knew little of it and could not offer Zen any advice.

Zen glanced at her and said, "Since you can't come with me and the Ear Mice are going to Stage Thirty-two, you should go with them."

"I... I'll wait for you here," said Libby.

"It's too dangerous here!" Fidel yelled in warning.

"Normally, you staying here wouldn't be a problem. But Fidel is right, the Soul Interdicting Water has begun flooding and who knows what followed the water in," Zen pointed out shaking his head as he spoke.

The Ghost-claw Worms alone were tough to deal with, not to mention there could be more than one kind of creature in the Soul Interdicting Water.

Libby considered this a while and decided Zen made a lot of sense and so she agreed.

Zen then jumped up straight to the first bone cave on the left and climbed up along the wall.

It was over ten thousand feet long and very wide. He could still hear the echo of his footsteps when he walked. When he was halfway up, a black fog appeared around the cave.

This gave him pause and he hesitated.

But then, the Primeval Lord of Heaven, who had been observing Zen this whole time, reminded him, "Don't worry. This black fog is only to scare off souls and can't harm a physical body."

Holy Souls were forbidden to step on this road, naturally there were some measures to stop them.

These words of comfort swept Zen's worries away and he continued climbing up.

He was almost at the top when a ray of light shone in front of him, lighting the dim cave.

"Does this bone cave lead outside?"

Zen's eyes glinted and he quickened his pace.

When he finally reached the top, he saw what it was like outside the bone cave...

He saw a boundless blue sea and slender bones in the water upside down, sticking out like bamboo growing in the sea. This was the forbidden area outside the bone caves that Libby had mentioned! Chapter 3769 Bone Slaves Once he was out of the bone cave, Zen saw a sprawling white beach in front of him.

He bent down to grab the white sand and watched it fall in between his fingers. "This sand is also bones. Were countless bones truly crushed and gathered here?"

"Ordinary crushed bones would have already been weathered. These bones were originally this small," the Primeval Lord of Heaven answered.

Hearing this, Zen lifted the sand on his palm and looked at it more carefully. As the Primeval Lord of Heaven said, these bones were indeed whole and were just incredibly small.

For such bones to be so small that they ended up covering an entire area and be mistaken for sand was both incredible and unsettling. "Are these from the tiny creatures of the Calculation Civilization?" Zen asked.

The green figure on the Civilization Artifact shook its head. "It's not us.

We're even way smaller than these bones."

Too many civilizations and creatures had existed in the chaos.

Over a thousand races had once become ruling civilizations and those underneath them, were even more numerous. Of course, there would always be creatures bigger or smaller than others.

"If you walk a bit more, you'll come upon some new discoveries," the Primeval Lord of Heaven said.

Zen decided to walk further along the beach and, to his surprise, found the bones that littered the ground progressively get larger. At first, it had been the size of a grain of sand until it became the size of a pea, then the size of a fist...

This somehow reminded him of the Immemorial Wilderness save for the fact that the bones there were randomly placed. Here on the beach, the bones were arranged in a certain orderly manner.

As he ventured forward, Zen began to see more familiar bones, specifically, human bones! He bent down and picked up a random arm bone. "The bone beach records all creatures on the Other Shore?"

"Yes," the Primeval Lord of Heaven confirmed.

Zen turned the bone in his hand curiously. "What about the Regal Jade Civilization?" he asked.

Some civilizations had special forms and the Regal Jade Civilization was one of them since they did not have any bones.

"Look at the front left," the Regal Jade Spirit suddenly said, with a smile on his face.

The Regal Jade Spirit had also stepped into the Land of Bone Tribulation before, so he knew some things.

Zen did as he said. When he looked to the left, he saw various green fragments in between the bones. Beside these fragments were metal bones from the Metal Civilization.

"Entering the Soul City allows one's soul to complete a transformation while entering the Land of Bone Tribulation allows one's body to undergo change. The degree of transformation of soul and body directly determines the power you will obtain in the Eternal Scroll Painting," the Primeval Lord of Heaven explained.

Eternal Warriors at the Eternal Realm were the most powerful existence in this world.

However, the Eternal Scroll Painting also had a ranking system and the higher one's ranking was, the greater power one would obtain.

Zen raised his eyebrows with interest. "The Eternal Scroll Painting?"

The Primeval Lord of Heaven nodded. "Yes. You've gotten nine Holy Soul Imprints..." he began. "You are the number-one person in history and just by relying on these nine Holy Soul Imprints, your ranking in the Eternal Scroll Painting won't be low. However, if you can obtain nine Bone Tribulation Imprints, then your ranking could naturally go higher!"

In fact, the Primeval Lord of Heaven already spoke to the elites of the human race about this. All of them had high expectations for Zen.

"The more imprints, the higher the ranking?" Zen surmised. It hadn't been that hard to figure out.

"Most cases go like that though there are exceptions," the Primeval Lord of Heaven said. "My junior fellow disciple obtained sixteen imprints but the ranking he received hadn't been ideal. The one who ranked first only had fourteen imprints."

More imprints meant a bigger advantage in the Eternal Scroll Painting but it wasn't the end-all and be-all of everything. There were always creatures with astonishing willpower that could create miracles and defeat those far stronger than them.

This piqued Zen's interest. "Then, who is it?" he asked.

A trace of caution appeared on the Primeval Lord of Heaven's face. "It's the Eye Spirit of the Element Spirit race."

There weren't many creatures that could make the Primeval Lord of Heaven so cautious but the Eye Spirit was one of them.

"Eye Spirit..." Zen repeated. "Is it the strongest warrior of the Element Spirit race?" The Primeval Lord of Heaven nodded grimly.

"Yes."

That was the only answer Zen needed and he stopped asking about the subject.

After passing through the Land of Bone Tribulation, he would enter Stage Thirty-two and then get into the Eternal Scroll Painting. Now though, he had to focus on getting through this beach of bones first.

After he passed by the human bones, the following bones all got bigger and bigger. Now, there were bones several dozen feet, further on they would get bigger until they were several hundred feet, and so on! Only a small part of these huge bones floated above the sea, leaving the rest under the waters.

Not long after, Zen finally arrived at the edge of the beach. Any further and he would be in the ocean of Soul Interdicting Water.

"It's the end. Where is the Land of Bone Tribulation?" he asked.

"Wait. There should be bone slaves coming," the Primeval Lord of Heaven told him.

Zen did as he was told and took a seat on one of the huge bones to wait. In the distance, dark green flames suddenly blazed to life.

'Ghost fire?' Zen thought to himself.

The cemetery was a place to bury bones and phosphorescent flames frequently rose due to the sheer amount of remains buried there. It was just a bit surprising that there would be flames that burned, though it was the daytime here.

As the flames rose, they floated towards the skulls that then gained sentience and began to look for the rest of their bodies.

Spine, shoulder blade, ribs...

A short while later, fully-formed and assembled human skeletons began to walk towards Zen.

"Are they the bone slaves you were talking about earlier?" Zen asked.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven nodded with a smile. "Yes. Every race will have their own bone slaves."

Zen nodded in understanding but a question suddenly popped in his head.

"What if a certain race enters this place for the first time?"

"Before they enter, the bones of their race will have been created and placed here," the Primeval Lord of Heaven explained patiently.

There were some special powers on the Other Shore. It should also be noted that the Soul City and the Land of Bone Tribulation were constructed by the Instant Civilization and were thus naturally different from other places.

Zen raised yet another question. "These bones... they were created out of nowhere then?"

The Primeval Lord of Heaven smiled, associating Zen's question with the Truth of Three-Energy Construction. "It is indeed possible!"

Ziya discovered the Truth of Three-Energy Construction outside the chaos, which meant the Instant Civilization also came from there.

The reanimated skeletons came straight to Zen and the first skeleton that passed him by flipped a slightly larger bone. Zen watched as the bone landed on the surface of the Soul Interdicting Water and transformed itself into a boat.

"Please get on," the skeleton said in a strange voice and gestured invitingly towards the boat.

A trace of vigilance appeared on Zen's face as he asked the Primeval Lord of Heaven's opinion in his mind.

"If you want to go to the Land of Bone Tribulation, then you naturally have to board this boat," the Primeval Lord of Heaven said, assuring Zen and comforting his nerves.

With no more reservations, Zen jumped and landed in the middle of the boat.

The other skeletons quickly got to work, scouring the ground for bones to be used as paddles and also getting on the boat.

Chapter 3770 Bone Island The white bone boat floated on the blue ocean.

It was rowed manually by the bone slaves, so it did not move too fast.

Zen possessed the ability to fly and could do so across the ocean, or even help the bone slaves speed up if he wished.

But the Primeval Lord of Heaven warned him not to break the rules of the Land of Bone Tribulation. They had entered the land in this way before. As per the advice he was given, Zen just watched on as the bone slaves paddled the boat forward slowly.

Their intelligence was at the most basic level, and although they were able to communicate smoothly with Zen, they seemed to know very little. When he asked of theirs and the Land of Bone Tribulation's origin, all they offered was dull, stiff answers.

After asking a few more questions, Zen gave up this pursuit with them.

Splash! Splash! Splash...

The boat continued on slowly, bypassing bones jutting out of the sea one by one, before Zen finally caught sight of a white island.

The island was made of thick bones piling up together and in the center was a huge skull, but Zen didn't know what creature it belonged to.

"Is this the Land of Bone Tribulation?" Zen asked.

"Yes," a bone slave nodded.

As the boat slowly approached the shore, Zen leaped casually into the air and landed on the island.

He stood firm when suddenly, a handful of sea water splashed at his head! Being on the Other Shore for so long, Zen was very alert to Soul Interdicting Water and the like. The thunder wings on his back exploded violently as his body turned away, barely avoiding the Soul Interdicting Water! He stabilized in midair and now saw clearly that there were more than a dozen creatures on both sides of the island! They were of many different shapes and sizes; some were tiny, some were as big and burly as giants. But it was obvious they were Other Shore creatures.

"Hasn't it been a long time since anyone entered the Land of Bone Tribulation?" Zen asked in confusion.

He thought he was the only one here. Seeing so many Other Shore creatures appear all of a sudden was certainly unexpected.

"Creatures in the chaos can't enter the Land of Bone Tribulation, but the Other Shore creatures can," the Primeval Lord of Heaven revealed to Zen.

As long as they were not stage rulers who were bound to a certain stage, the creatures of the Other Shore were also capable of becoming stronger, gaining the Holy Soul, receiving the training in the Land of Bone Tribulation and entering the Eternal Scroll Painting to get to Stage Thirtythree.

"It's that human brat!"

"Human, don't you know the rules? Those from outside the Other Shore must be tainted with the Soul Interdicting Water before they can land!"

"Yes, it's a rule. We'll let you down after you bath in the Soul Interdicting Water!"

The Land of Bone Tribulation was more difficult to pass through and would take more time than the Soul City.

These Other Shore creatures had been here a long time and had become familiar with each other. Ganging up against outsiders was easy for them.

Unfortunately, Zen was quite clearly an outsider.

"Rules? Who made these rules?" Zen asked narrowing his eyes slightly.

"No one made them, this has always been the way in the Land of Bone Tribulation," explained an Other Shore creature.

"Ha-ha," Zen laughed coldly. "No one in the chaos has been able to enter here after ancient times, and still, after so long, this rule has not been abolished? Or is it that you made it up just now?"

The Soul Interdicting Water only had an effect on the creatures outside the Other Shore. This rule was clearly intended for the creatures in chaos. But it had been quite a long time since any of them stepped into this land.

Why did the rule come back just as Zen had appeared? This must be the doing of the Element Spirit race.

Zen's question left the Other Shore creatures speechless.

"The only reason why you sprayed the Soul Interdicting Water on me is to prevent me from escaping, am I right?" he asked, slowly descending as the Other Shore Power within the Civilization Artifact surged crazily in his inner world.

Splash! The Other Shore Power erupted and sent his body smashing down towards the island like a meteorite falling from the sky.

The Other Shore creatures had intended to surround Zen, but when they felt the speed at which he had fallen, they all wore stunned expressions and rushed backwards.

Boom! Zen slammed into the island.

Under the immense power, the entire island began shaking violently and spreading mini tsunamis out over the surrounding sea.

Zen looked at the ground in surprise. It too was made of bones, but they were tough far beyond his expectations. There wasn't even a hint of damage to them from his impact! He might not have shattered the bones, but instead shattered the confidence of the Other Shore creatures.

It seemed it was as Zen had guessed; they had indeed received news that a creature from the chaos was on his way and if they captured him, their races would be rewarded handsomely.

They had expected the creature from the chaos would be weak and an easy capture if they took advantage of the Soul Interdicting Water, as long as he was off guard. They certainly had not expected him to possess such incredible strength.

They were stunned silent and lowered their heads like children being reprimanded by their parents.

After all, they were not creatures from the chaos and could not leave the Other Shore. Surrendering was their best option when faced with a far stronger warrior.

"Does anyone else want to sprinkle the Soul Interdicting Water on me?"

Zen asked menacingly as he scanned the creatures around.

No one answered. They just looked at Zen with reverence.

Zen walked towards a burly creature. He had the head of a bull and a pair of sharp horns. He was from the Sturdy Bull race residing in Stage Twentyseven. Seeing Zen heading straight for him, the Sturdy Bull quickly explained in a panic, "He told us the news. He came here and told us that if we attacked you, the Element Spirit race would reward us, which would benefit our race!"

The Sturdy Bull pointed at a cat-like creature not far off.

The cat-like creature took two steps back when he was pointed out. His eyes narrowed and gazed dangerously, ready to deal with Zen's attack at any moment.

But Zen just glanced at him indifferently and said, "I came here to pass the Land of Bone Tribulation. As for the grudge between me and the Element Spirit race, you'd better stay out of it!"

These Other Shore creatures were also outstanding warriors of their different races. They had thought Zen was a weak lamb they could bully, and naturally they wanted to rush forward to capture him.

But Zen displayed such great power that they decided it was better to not risk their lives! "Yes, yes. I'm not a member of the Element Spirit race," the Sturdy Bull nodded.

They immediately let out a sigh of relief and all the tension in the atmosphere relaxed when Zen showed restrained hostility.

Zen looked into the depths of the island and asked, "Has the Land of Bone Tribulation opened yet?"

On the bone boat, the Primeval Lord of Heaven had told him the basics rules of the Land of Bone Tribulation.

Like the Soul City, the Land of Bone Tribulation also opened for a period of time and then closed for another period of time. But the periods were much longer than that of the Soul City.

Chapter 3771 Myriad Tribulations Storm The skull that occupied three fourths of the island was in fact the entrance to the Land of Bone Tribulation.

"The Land of Bone Tribulation opens every eight hundred hours. Six hundred and forty hours have now passed," the Sturdy Bull replied.

"So it will open in seven days?" asked Zen.

"Yes!" The Sturdy Bull answered.

Seven days...

Zen pondered this a while and decided not to leave the Other Shore.

These Other Shore creatures were not reliable. If he left, there was no guarantee they wouldn't set up arrays and wait for an opportunity to strike at him...

He sat down cross-legged facing the skull, dead still in meditation, waiting for its opening.

The Other Shore creatures stood behind him, sizing him up silently. They didn't want to provoke him anymore and so waited with him.

Seven days passed by quickly.

Once it had been eight hundred hours, the huge skull trembled and began rising slowly.

Zen sensed the change and opened his eyes, staring intently at the rising skull before him.

He now realized it was a complete skull but the lower end of it had been buried in the island before.

As it continued to rise, more and more was revealed and a cervical spine now became visible; it turned out to be a complete skeleton! Crack! Crack! Crack! Once the skull had risen a fair bit, a strange sound echoed from between its jaws. Its mouth slowly opened, releasing, incredibly, a pathway.

The Other Shore creatures itched to give it a go. When the Land of Bone Tribulation had opened before, they would swarm in.

But this time, as Zen stood at the front, none of them dared to move first.

Zen walked without hesitation, straight into the large mouth of the skull.

The Other Shore creatures followed in as soon as he entered.

Inside the skull were stairs made of thin bones. After walking down the bone stairs, they returned to the bottom of the sea. Then another wondrous scene was revealed to them.

The Soul Interdicting Water with dark blue light was blocked by an invisible force, forming isolation walls.

In the center were many floating white bone plates.

This was Zen's first time entering, so he stood on the stairs and looked at the bone plates carefully.

The Other Shore creatures behind him dared not to force him further, so all they could do was wait silently. Zen watched the plates for a full five minutes before they could not wait any longer. After all, time was precious when the Land of Bone Tribulation opened.

"Human friend, you should sit on the white bone plate first to enter the Land of Bone Tribulation," the Sturdy Bull said from behind.

Zen smiled faintly, sensing the angst among these creatures. He jumped down from the stairs and landed on one of the bone plates.

Whoosh! The moment he set foot on it, the bone plate carried him to the side.

The other creatures jumped onto the bone plates too and sat down, also retreating to the side.

Once they all sat on bone plates, identical bone plates appeared on the opposite side with skeletons placed on them.

On the plate opposite to the Sturdy Bull, was a huge skeleton similar to him.

On the plate opposite to Zen, was a human skeleton, the same size as he was, making the same moves he did.

Zen raised his hand and so did the opposing skeleton.

Zen turned his head, and so did the skeleton...

It seemed to be a mirror image, but with no flesh and blood-it was just a pale white human skeleton.

"Is this my tribulation skeleton?" Zen asked, staring at the skeleton.

In the Land of Bone Tribulation, everyone had their own corresponding tribulation skeletons. When they accepted the test of the land, their tribulation skeletons would in turn undergo a significant change.

Zen's tribulation skeleton had just been born when he had entered, so it was as white as white jade.

But the huge tribulation skeleton corresponding to the Sturdy Bull was covered with a faint layer of golden glaze. He had been here for a long time and clearly had gained a lot.

However, this was all gained for the tribulation skeleton. Before it merged with him, he had gained nothing on his own body.

Although these creatures had been here a long time, they still did not possess the ability to compete with Zen! "Your tribulation skeleton is too new," the Sturdy Bull said with a trace of pride. He looked at his own tribulation skeleton, which shone with golden light, with love glinting in his eyes. He finally had something to be proud of in front of Zen The other creatures shared the same sentiment. They didn't know what Zen had done to obtain control of that amazing power, but what did that matter? Here, he was still a newcomer! Once they obtained the Myriad Tribulations Body, their strength would still be able to surpass Zen's! Zen's eyes flashed with mockery as he asked, "How long have you cultivated here?"

"I've been here only seven years. I've reached this level quite fast actually!"

the Sturdy Bull admitted confidently.

"Yes. Brice is quite talented, mainly because he has a divine body which is stronger than other creatures' from the moment he was born," said an Other Shore creature. He then pointed to a centipede-shaped creature close by.

"That long insect there is even stranger. He has cultivated a unique body refining method. In just a year, he has already entered the sixteenth layer of the Myriad Tribulations Storm!"

The surface of that centipede's tribulation skeleton shone with golden light as well. It was almost a Myriad Tribulations Body! The centipede had been silent this whole time, lying motionless on his own bone plate. He was focused solely on cultivating the Myriad Tribulations Body and had no interest whatsoever in other matters. Even when the Element Spirit race had sent a message to attack Zen, he paid it no mind.

As they spoke, an intense pressure overtook the entire space, suddenly expanding and contracting along with the violent rising and falling of the surrounding sea water. A storm had formed in the center! The storm rose and swept out the Soul Interdicting Water from the surrounding "walls".

Drops of Soul Interdicting Water gathered in the center of the storm.

Zen was inevitably hit by the Soul Interdicting Water as he sat on the bone plate.

He tried to dodge, but the Soul Interdicting Water was too dense. He was hit and then gave up trying to dodge it. He had accepted that he was unable to leave the Other Shore.

Buzz! The Soul Interdicting Water was completely submerged in the rising storm, forming a larger blue storm.

'Is this the Myriad Tribulations Storm?' Frowning, Zen looked at the scene unfolding in front of him. At the same time, he felt confused as to whether he should refine his body with the Soul Interdicting Water.

When he was still at a loss for what his next move should be, streaks of golden liquid suddenly rose from the bottom of the storm.

Feeling the aura of the golden liquid shrank his pupils. Even the Primeval Lord of Heaven who was observing in his inner world seemed to remember something, which changed his face in an instant! Chapter 3772 The Tearing Force The golden liquid's aura was quite similar to that of the Descending Rings.

Not long ago, Fuxi and the Snake Goddess from the Source World personally asked Zen for the golden red Chaotic Source Spirits. When they were used together with the Descending Rings, they could directly summon anything from the Other Shore down to the chaos. It was a way equivalent to breaking the restrictions of truth! In fact, the Primeval Lord of Heaven also knew that there would be a bluegolden storm in the Land of Bone Tribulation.

The blue was the Soul Interdicting Water, but so far, no one knew what the golden liquid was.

However, it had been a long time since the Primeval Lord of Heaven was in the Land of Bone Tribulation, and he had long forgotten about the aura of this golden liquid.

That was why he couldn't connect them to the Land of Bone Tribulation at all when he saw Zen's golden red Chaotic Source Spirits before.

But now that Zen had entered the Land of Bone Tribulation, he and Zen naturally realized immediately what the golden liquid might be. "Primeval Lord of Heaven, why is this golden liquid's aura in this storm the same as the aura of the Descending Rings?" asked Zen.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven was lost in thought. There was a somewhat strange connection between the two.

The Myriad Tribulations Storm was a great test for warriors who entered it for training, and only those strong-willed enough could pass it.

The mixture of the golden liquid and the Soul Interdicting Water could cause a violent stab of pain to anyone it hit.

It was so painful that even the Primeval Lord of Heaven still clearly remembered how it felt when he experienced it over a thousand chaotic eras ago. "If the golden liquid is the same type of thing as the Descending Rings, then it is used to summon things from the Other Shore, while the Soul Interdicting Water works to prevent anything from descending..." Zen analyzed.

Upon hearing Zen's words, the Primeval Lord of Heaven broke free from his train of thought. He suddenly perked up and said, "I got it. It turns out that the Land of Bone Tribulation is so ingeniously designed.

The Instant Civilization was smart to make use of the geographical advantages..." "What geographical advantages?" Zen asked curiously.

"As you said, the Soul Interdicting Water prevents things from descending while the golden liquid works the same as the Descending Ring, which is used to summon things down. Their functions contrast each other. If they appear at the same time, then the Myriad Tribulations Storm, which could tear almost everything apart, is formed," the Primeval Lord of Heaven theorized.

Back then, he couldn't figure out why the mixture of the Soul Interdicting Water and the golden liquid could have such an effect.

Now, he seemed to have completely understood it.

The two types of liquid within the storm were like two hands: one hand extended to the Other Shore, while the other extended outside the Other Shore. Naturally, a powerful tearing force was produced.

"I'll go in first!" the centipede declared before he and his bone plate entered the Myriad Tribulations Storm in the center.

At the same time, the tribulation skeleton on his opposite side followed suit.

It entered the Myriad Tribulations Storm from the other side of the storm! "Da! Da! Da!"

Countless drops of blue and gold mixed together and floated inside the Myriad Tribulations Storm. When the droplets hit a body, they exploded and produced numerous strange black cracks. The cracks expanded, then released a powerful tearing force.

If the droplets hit a body that wasn't cultivated to perfection, then it would be quickly torn apart! As the centipede continued to advance, the tribulation skeleton on his opposite side also moved towards the center of the Myriad Tribulations Storm.

The small water drops in the outermost layer of the Myriad Tribulations Storm were very small and sparsely scattered. About ten feet deeper inside, however, the small water drops grew bigger and became denser. When viewed from the outside, there was a layer of water drops every ten feet— and there was a total of twenty layers from the outermost part to the center of the storm! After the centipede was thirty feet deep into the Myriad Tribulations Storm, small rings suddenly appeared on the surface of his body. The rings were tightly locked together and increased the centipede's physical strength.

"Da! Da! Da!"

In turn, the rings blocked all the black cracks the small water drops made on his body.

Meanwhile, his tribulation skeleton on the other side experienced the same as well. As a result, the tribulation skeleton glowed a golden light after the storm repeatedly hit his body.

The water drops at the outermost layer did not affect the tribulation skeleton at all, so the centipede had no choice but to go deeper into the storm every time the Land of Bone Tribulation opened.

As he moved forward with ease, he abruptly stopped in the sixteenth layer and remained motionless right after. His tribulation skeleton also stopped in the sixteenth layer on the other side.

Of course, all the Other Shore creatures who saw the centipede move so quickly sported envious looks.

"It seemed that he can easily withstand sixteen layers of the Myriad Tribulations Storm with the help of the tribulation skeleton…"

"I don't know when I can reach the same level!"

"My tribulation skeleton has just entered the third layer..."

The Other Shore creatures began to discuss among themselves as they drove their bone plates forward and entered the Myriad Tribulations Storm.

Generally speaking, one's tribulation skeleton became stronger after they entered the Myriad Tribulations Storm. It also affected their real bodies' strength, so it meant that they could advance further after that process.

But after one got out of the Myriad Tribulations Storm their tribulation skeletons and their real bodies were no longer connected. Only after they had truly obtained the Myriad Tribulations Bodies would their tribulation skeletons and their real bodies finally merge.

Once all the Other Shore creatures had entered, Zen also took control of his bone plate and entered the Myriad Tribulations Storm.

"Da!"

A blue-golden drop of water hit his right arm first and burst into a black crack. His body slightly trembled.

Indeed, the tearing force from that small water drop was powerful! Fortunately, he had absorbed a large amount of Body-strengthening Jades and his physical body had reached its limit, so he was strong enough to take it. Furthermore, he wasn't afraid of anything because he had the Chaotic Source Spirits to protect his body. Thus, he simply continued to drive the bone plate forward.

On the other hand, the Other Shore creatures in the Myriad Tribulations Storm all looked at him.

As for them, they all activated their body protecting theurgies to defend against the water droplets. Some of them used illusory shield shadows that surrounded their bodies, while some others' bodies glowed with a golden light. While all of them changed in some way, there were no changes in Zen's body at all.

"Did that guy just withstand the water drops with his physical body?"

"Will he really go to the second layer the first time he has entered the storm? He's so aggressive!"

"Just wait and see, he'll surely suffer!"

It was known that the water drops were immensely powerful despite their size. It was likely for one to lose their life if they weren't careful in the Myriad Tribulations Storm.

Some of the Other Shore creatures even began to think that if Zen was seriously injured, they wouldn't mind killing him. They became more excited now that the Soul Interdicting Water had tainted Zen, since he would have no way to escape! But just as the crowd thought, Zen had already driven the bone plate thirty feet forward and stepped into the third layer.

On the other side, his tribulation skeleton also sat upright on the bone plate.

The water droplets continuously hit it, but there were only faint golden marks on its surface.

"Even though these small water drops have a strong tearing force, it cannot affect my body on a large scale. Warriors at the Chaotic Source Realm are best at resisting such attacks," Zen said in a low voice.

The Chaotic Source Spirits feared bearing too much power at once the most. However, the constant tearing of the water droplets hardly exhausted them.

Zen looked ahead and the corner of his mouth slightly curled up. Then, he did something that surprised everyone around him.

He leaned forward a little, then the bone plate quickly moved forward. In the blink of an eye, he was already a hundred feet into the storm and had landed at the side of the warrior from the Sturdy Bull race! Chapter 3773 Too Slow The member of the Sturdy Bull race still focused on resisting the water drops. His muscles flashed with a bronze glow.

Every time he activated his bloodline theurgy, his blood vitality became more potent and greatly increased the toughness of his physical body.

"I need to hold on for six hours!" he exclaimed.

As long as he stayed within the tenth layer for six full hours, his tribulation skeleton would surely grow stronger.

However, to do so was a huge challenge. After all, to continuously activate the bloodline power consumed a lot of his strength.

Fortunately, the current round of Myriad Tribulations Storm had just started. He was still full of energy, so the task was a piece of cake.

Just as he sat down and turned around to check how the human newcomer was doing, he suddenly realized that Zen was already at the spot beside him.

His eyes widened to the size of saucers. He stared blankly at Zen for a long while before he came back to his senses.

"How is this possible?"

He was so shocked as if he had seen a monster and not a human. He couldn't figure out how Zen had reached the spot beside him in such a short period! They were already a hundred feet into the Myriad Tribulations Storm at that point, and the water drops in the tenth layer were far more powerful. It was simply impossible, even if one's physical body had absorbed enough Bodystrengthening Jades and had cultivated to its limit! What made it more surprising was that it was Zen's first time to experience such a trial, and his tribulation skeleton hardly even bore any damages! With a steady drip, the water drops kept hitting Zen's body.

Black cracks spread all over his skin, but it looked like he wasn't in pain at all.

Opposite him on the other side of the Myriad Tribulations Storm, the water droplets had quickly tempered his tribulation skeleton.

The closer they got to the center of the storm, the faster the tribulation skeleton would be refined.

The refinement speed at the tenth layer was a hundred times faster than that in the outermost layer! As the small drops of water poured continuously onto Zen's tribulation skeleton, its golden color became increasingly clear.

"This is..."

Then, it glowed brighter while he felt his body become solid and stable as if an invisible power had enhanced it.

"Is this feeling from my tribulation skeleton?" Zen muttered with raised brows. Of course, he was a bit surprised.

He was different from the Other Shore races, like the Sturdy Bull race.

After all, he could withstand the Myriad Tribulations Storm with merely the help of the Chaotic Source Spirits.

In fact, had it been ordinary Chaotic Source Realm warriors, it wouldn't be long before the water droplets had exhausted their Chaotic Source Spirits.

Thanks to the special Truth of Godly Way Zen had obtained, his Chaotic Source Spirits recovered quickly after an attack.

That was why he could easily survive in the Myriad Tribulations Storm.

"You, you... How did you resist the water drops?" the Sturdy Bull couldn't help but ask curiously.

"With my physical body, of course," replied Zen.

The Sturdy Bull's face twitched as he was rendered speechless.

The Sturdy Bull race was an Other Shore race that only appeared in recent chaotic eras. They didn't know much about the human race, and most of their curiosity came from the sudden increase of human Souls of Light on the Other Shore in later years.

However, they still didn't take the human Souls of Light at the Holy Soul Realm seriously. After all, even though the Holy Souls were strong enough to fight against the Other Shore creatures, the Other Shore creatures could still become much stronger if they cultivated a Myriad Tribulations Body.

However, contrary to the rumors, not only did Zen have a physical form, he also had too much power that was beyond what the Sturdy Bull had imagined! While the member of the Sturdy Bull race was still in shock, Zen suddenly asked, "It seems that the refinement speed in the tenth layer isn't fast. How long will it take to achieve the same level of your tribulation skeleton?"

Zen's dissatisfaction at the refining speed in the tenth layer stunned the Sturdy Bull once again. He remained quiet for a while before he said, "It will take you at least a couple of months. Every time the Land of Bone Tribulation opened, I held on for five hours in the tenth layer. I have spent about a total of three months here already!"

Generally speaking, the time between the openings of the Land of Bone Tribulation was very long. Even if the Sturdy Bull activated his bloodline power to its limit, he could only hold on for five hours to six hours at most.

However, he still stayed in the eighth or ninth layer to refine his tribulation skeleton even after he had already exhausted his bloodline power. He didn't leave until the Land of Bone Tribulation was closed.

"Three months... That's too much time for me!" Zen said and shook his head.

After that, he suddenly drove the bone plate beneath his feet forward.

It turned out that he directly crossed the tenth layer and entered the eleventh layer! The water drops in the eleventh layer were much more violent, and the black cracks that appeared on Zen's skin grew wider. His Chaotic Source Spirits became twice as exhausted, but the refining speed of the tribulation skeleton also increased several times! The member of the Sturdy Bull race clearly knew the benefits of entering the eleventh layer. Once one was strong enough to withstand the water droplets in the eleventh layer, their cultivation speed would greatly increase.

However, it was already hard for him to stay in the tenth layer for six hours due to his current strength. He wondered if he could hold on for even five minutes in the eleventh layer.

In the end, he decided not to enter the eleventh layer before his tribulation skeleton reached a higher level.

On the other hand, Zen barely spent time in the tenth layer before he advanced further into the eleventh layer. Was his body strong enough to withstand the water drops' rapidly increasing power? "Easy does it, my friend. The difficulty of the eleventh layer is..." Before the member of the Sturdy Bull race could finish his warning, Zen had arrived steadily at the eleventh layer.

He looked back at the member of the Sturdy Bull race and said, "Sorry.

What was that you said?"

"It's nothing... Never mind." The Sturdy Bull waved his hands and smiled awkwardly. He realized that his worries were completely unnecessary.

The tribulation skeleton's refining speed in the eleventh layer increased greatly, and at the same time, the pressure Zen felt also intensified by several degrees. Even so, the exhaustion of the Chaotic Source Spirits was still within his control.

At that moment, all the remaining Other Shore creatures in the Myriad Tribulations Storm observed Zen and started to discuss among themselves.

"How is this possible?"

"Even if he cultivates some special theurgy, he won't be able to hold on for long, right?"

"You should know that his tribulation skeleton hasn't grown so strong to protect his body!"

Even the centipede that fully concentrated on his cultivation in the sixteenth layer turned his head, his eyes filled with bewilderment and uncertainty.

The centipede had reached his current level through step-by-step improvement.

His physical body was already strong enough to bear the water drops in the outer layers, so his tribulation skeleton could grow stronger much faster. In turn, his enhanced tribulation skeleton served as additional protection as he advanced further.

However, Zen had rushed into the eleventh layer even though he hardly spent time in the outer layers. His tribulation skeleton was barely refined, so it couldn't support him at all.

If the centipede stayed in the eleventh layer without the protection of the tribulation skeleton, he wouldn't be able to withstand the water drops! Most of the Other Shore creatures who bet that Zen wouldn't be able to stay long in the eleventh layer were indeed right. It had only been five minutes since he had arrived there, but he already felt dissatisfied with the refining speed in the eleventh layer.

Chapter 3774 Sudden Change With everyone looking on, Zen drove the bone plate forward once more.

He passed the twelfth layer.

The thirteenth layer...

The fourteenth layer...

The fifteenth layer...

The sixteenth layer...

He moved inwards for a hundred and sixty feet and finally arrived beside the centipede-like creature.

Crack! Crack! Crack! Crack! The small water drops within the sixteenth layer rained down hard on Zen like a violent storm.

His whole body was wrapped in the black cracks that tore wildly at his body.

The Chaotic Source Spirits in his body continued to absorb the battering he took, but they dimmed fast at the same time.

As the Chaotic Source Spirits dimmed, the Truth of Godly Way continued to gush out. The warm current was like the water of an oasis in a desert, nourishing everything it flowed over.

Before the Chaotic Source Spirits fell into absolute fatigue, the Truth of Godly Way had already restored them.

'I'll stay here!' Zen thought to himself, assessing the situation.

This was a point of perfect balance for him.

If he continued onward, his Chaotic Source Spirits might not be able to withstand the force. Once they were fatigued, Zen would not be able to hold on much longer.

And on the sixteenth layer, he could not only refine his tribulation skeleton quickly, but he could also cultivate the Chaotic Source Spirits at the same time! Crack! Crack! Crack! Countless small drops of water fell on the surface of his tribulation skeleton, and wisps of golden light swiftly covered it.

Passing the trial of the Land of Bone Tribulation usually took a long time because the tribulation skeleton would only begin refining on the outermost layer. But as the refining effect was so unsatisfactory on the outer layers, it would take a long time surely to complete the trial.

In fact, from the sixteenth layer onward, the speed of refining would increase greatly! "He... What the hell is he?"

"He went straight to the sixteenth layer!"

"If I were there, I'm afraid those little water drops would tear me apart!"

They had just been thinking Zen wouldn't last long on the eleventh layer, yet now he stood steadily on the sixteenth layer. Getting there would take most of them a great deal of time but he did it in an instant! His speed stunned the Other Shore creatures to their core...

"Is this real?"

"How ridiculous!"

"I finally understand why the Element Spirit race wants him dealt with!"

Such rapid growth would pose a terrible threat to anyone.

When the centipede stared at Zen, the rings on his body began to crack! His cultivation method relied on his extremely powerful belief.

The stronger his confidence was in himself, the stronger the protection power of the rings would be! With the help of this theurgy, the centipede, like Zen, had also crossed the first six layers in an instant and entered directly into the seventh layer for cultivation. His speed was clearly far beyond the others.

This gave him massive confidence, making him feel as though he was the most talented there was. Thus, the power of his rings was greatly increased.

Soon, after his tribulation skeleton grew stronger, he would be able to enter the seventeenth layer! If he then passed another three layers, he would be able to obtain the Myriad Tribulations Body. Imagining how powerful he would become once he fused with his tribulation skeleton excited him a whole lot.

The centipede was silent not because this was his personality, but because he felt that he was special and decided not to communicate with the others.

It was true the others that entered the Land of Bone Tribulation were also outstanding in their respective races, but he was still above them.

Now however, Zen had brutally shattered his stable and confident state of mind.

It was his first time in the Land of Bone Tribulation, and yet here he was, on the same layer as he was! Such a talent was unheard of! The centipede cried out in his heart continuously.

No matter how hard he tried to deny this, even closing his eyes again and again in the hope it wasn't real, Zen was still sitting steadily beside him.

The undeniable fact that he was not the greatest ever began to discourage the centipede. His cultivation method had its flaw and cracks began appearing on the rings.

Seeing that his theurgy was no longer able to help him resist the small water drops of the sixteenth layer, he had no choice but to retreat back ten feet and enter the fifteenth layer.

Crack! Crack! Crack! Crack! But even the water drops of the fifteenth layer still tore his rings and forced him to continue his retreat.

On the fourteenth layer, he retreated again...

On the thirteenth layer, he retreated again...

On the twelfth layer, he retreated again...

He finally stopped on the eleventh layer, only ten feet away from the Sturdy Bull.

The centipede's downfall attracted the whispers of the other creatures.

They had cultivated together for so long and knew what kind of theurgy they each used.

They also knew that the centipede's body protection theurgy was connected to his state of mind. It seemed that Zen's performance had dealt a heavy blow to the centipede.

Of course, Zen didn't know he had unwittingly made the centipede retreat again and again.

After maintaining balance, Zen also calmed down and sat upright on the bone plate to be baptized by small drops of water.

One day passed.

Two days passed.

Three days passed...

In the Myriad Tribulations Storm, all that could be heard was the patter of the small drops of water that smashed onto everyone's body.

Occasionally, when the Other Shore creatures couldn't bear it, they would retreat ten feet. If they felt that their condition had improved, they would advance back ten feet.

When the centipede was on the eleventh layer, he did a lot of self-reflection and after calming down, he advanced twenty feet and entered the thirteenth layer once more.

Ten days passed...

Twenty days passed...

The Chaotic Source Spirits in Zen's body had experienced an unprecedented torture.

At the same time being repaired by the Truth of Godly Way, the Chaotic Source Spirits didn't take a break...

Zen had often performed this kind of oppression after he came out of the Chaotic Source World. It was thanks to this method he was able to step into the later stage of the Chaotic Source Realm in such a short period of time! However, after staying in the Myriad Tribulations Storm for twenty-eight days, his Chaotic Source Spirits finally encountered some issues.

They had integrated into his body and suddenly disappeared and changed into another form. This process caused them to no longer absorb energy for him! Crack! Crack! Crack! Crack! When the tiny water drops struck the surface of his body, it immediately caused a terribly intense pain! "What's going on?"

The pain had shocked Zen.

He had no choice but to protect his head with both hands and drive the bone plate to retreat.

His body had originally been as sturdy as a weapon. Moreover, in the past nearly a month, the tribulation skeleton had been greatly enhanced to protect him.

If not for this, the moment the Chaotic Source Spirits disappeared, the black cracks that the small water drops created would have torn him to pieces! After retreating to the outermost layer of the Myriad Tribulations Storm, Zen stopped.

The surface of his body looked horrible and was covered in wounds caused by the black cracks that burst out.

Chapter 3775 Division Zen appeared to be grievously injured, but in truth, the damage was only skin deep. The water drops did not hurt his muscles and bones.

Circles of green light blossomed on Zen's body, and the surface-level wounds began to heal rapidly.

The Other Shore creatures saw what was happening, and they were dumbfounded at Zen's quick recovery.

Zen had persisted for almost a month, while most of the Other Shore creatures retreated again and again. Zen had been staying on the sixteenth layer to receive training, and the others all reluctantly agreed that Zen seemed to have gotten used to the sixteenth layer at this point.

They didn't expect that in the last few days, Zen would actually leave the Myriad Tribulations Storm, and he appeared to be injured.

"Is there something wrong with his method of body protection?"

"Perhaps..."

"Hey. It's clearly good enough for him to hold on for this long at the sixteenth layer. His tribulation skeleton has already surpassed many of ours!"

Even if Zen left awkwardly right now, what he had already accomplished was enough for them to recognize him as an extraordinary warrior.

After all, everyone relied on the method of body protection to stay within the Myriad Tribulations Storm. Although they couldn't see what method Zen had used to protect his body, it was already quite astonishing that he had held on for almost a month.

The green light shimmered and bloomed, spreading along the surface of Zen's body. After about five minutes, Zen's body returned to normal.

Zen, for his part, was less concerned about his own bodily injuries than about the Chaotic Source Spirits.

"There seems to be something wrong with the Chaotic Source Spirits," Zen murmured, frowning.

"What's wrong?" asked the Primeval Lord of Heaven.

"I am unable to detect their existence," replied Zen. He sought to sound calm, but he was deeply concerned.

Previously, he had been able to clearly sense the Chaotic Source Spirits scattered within his body. Now, however, it seemed that the Chaotic Source Spirits within him had vanished entirely. No matter how he probed, he could not sense them.

"How could that happen?" the Primeval Lord of Heaven asked curiously.

The Chaotic Source Spirits were special. They had been a subject of study for the Primeval Lord of Heaven, and the Snake Goddess had been able to use them through information hidden in the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed.

However, despite his extensive study, even the Primeval Lord of Heaven hadn't completely understood the Chaotic Source Spirits. The vast majority of people wouldn't be able to advance when they reached the late stage of the Chaotic Source Realm.

Even Athemar and Elizabeth would find twenty thousand divine megatons of power almost too much to be endured. If they wanted to bear a greater amount of power, it could be done only through a special bloodline theurgy or body protection theurgy.

However, since they couldn't cultivate the Myriad Tribulations Body, the bodies of the Chaotic Source Realm warriors were not strong enough.

Therefore, there was still an enormous gap between the talented warriors like Auden and Pearce, and the powerful masters like Yasamin and Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

On the other hand, Zen was something entirely unprecedented. He was probably the first person to step into the Land of Bone Tribulation after fusing with the Chaotic Source Spirits. He didn't expect that such a thing would happen this time.

"I'll check again," said Zen.

If he had truly lost the Chaotic Source Spirits, it would lead to a drastic reduction in his level of strength.

Without the help of the Chaotic Source Spirits, even if one possessed a Civilization Artifact, the power that they could unleash would be limited.

The situation would be different if the Inheritance of World was activated.

However, the Inheritance of World would also cause the Civilization Artifact to consume a lot of energy. It was impossible to keep using it continuously during each battle.

Zen carefully searched within himself, and finally sensed what was wrong.

His body was full of tiny light dots, each no larger than the point of a needle. The light dots had been too small for Zen to notice them without paying close attention. Now, as he probed further, he realized that the light dots were like grains of dust spreading throughout his body.

"Are these the light dots of the Chaotic Source Spirits which have disappeared? Why have they become so small?" Zen wondered, feeling stunned at his discovery.

It seemed that the light dots of the Chaotic Source Spirits had become abnormally small, and yet they had also multiplied in number. Listening, the Primeval Lord of Heaven was also confused, for he had not heard of such a thing happening before.

'The golden liquid in the Myriad Tribulations Storm is related to the Descending Rings, and the Descending Rings went to the Source World along with the Chaotic Source Spirits. There must be some connection, ' he thought.

"Zen, try using these tiny light dots the same way you always use the Chaotic Source Spirits. See if they can help you withstand the power,"

suggested the Primeval Lord of Heaven.

Everything on the Other Shore could provide some divine megatons of power, but the amount of power the Chaotic Source Spirits provided was a minus.

The Primeval Lord of Heaven theorized that everything on the Other Shore was simply a projection of energy from the Abstruse Energy World. In his theory, the Chaotic Source Spirits projected all the energy they had absorbed to a certain place in the Abstruse Energy World.

Of course, he was merely speculating, but he was interested in what Zen's predicament could reveal about his theory.

Zen nodded. "All right, I'll give it a try," he said.

He drove the bone plate again and entered the Myriad Tribulations Storm.

Even without the help of the Chaotic Source Spirits, Zen was capable of enduring the first layer without sustaining too much damage. At this point, he had been cultivating on the sixteenth layer for nearly a month. With his own tribulation skeleton he would still be able to enter the seventh or eighth layer.

But his intention now was just to test the tiny light dots. It wouldn't be necessary to advance to the higher layers.

He immediately felt the vivid blue and golden droplets on his skin.

In the outermost layer of the Myriad Tribulations Storm, the water drops were sparse, and the power of the black cracks that appeared on Zen's body was much weaker.

He paid little attention to the cracks. Instead, he turned his focus to the light dots within his body.

As a drop of blue and gold water hit Zen's skin, the tiny light dots in that area vibrated, and then were extinguished.

"They are fatigued,"

Zen said to himself, feeling helpless.

As the light dots got tired, the Truth of Godly Way produced by his physical body circulated within him. When it reached the affected light dots, they lit up again like stars.

However, as soon as they began glowing, another small drop of water hit Zen's skin, and the light dots immediately died down again.

These minuscule light dots were constantly getting tired and getting rejuvenated, in a nonstop cycle.

Zen realized that he would have to go through the entire Chaotic Source Realm again.

"I've already stepped into the late stage of the Chaotic Source Realm. Have I made use of these Chaotic Source Spirits to the limit?" Zen asked.

"Of course not," the Primeval Lord of Heaven answered quickly.

In the Source World, there were many powerful Chaotic Source Realm warriors, and each of them was countless times older than Zen. When these warriors cultivated to the late stage of the realm, they all stopped, unable to make any further progress. But they hadn't encountered a situation similar to Zen's.

"Then there are two conditions," Zen said. "The warriors have to cultivate to the late stage of the Chaotic Source Realm. And they also need to receive the training of the Myriad Tribulations Storm. Right?"

"That's possible," the Primeval Lord of Heaven said.

He thought that based on Zen's experience, it seemed that the Chaotic Source Spirits had completed a round of division! After the fission, it looked like the number of Chaotic Source Spirits in Zen's body had increased by a huge amount.

If these Chaotic Source Spirits could grow stronger, and Zen entered the late stage of the Chaotic Source Realm again, would his physical body be able to bear much more divine megatons of force? "What if you cultivate to the late stage of the Chaotic Source Realm again, and let the Chaotic Source Spirits split up one more time?"

suggested the Primeval Lord of Heaven. At his words, Zen's eyes lit up.

If the Chaotic Source Spirits continued to divide infinitely like this, his physical strength would probably increase to a terrifying level! It seemed that he would have to stay in the Myriad Tribulations Storm for longer than he had anticipated.

Chapter 3776 Temporary Closure Once the Land of Bone Tribulation was opened, the warriors had a training time of eight hundred hours. That was nearly a month.

But now that only fifty hours remained, Zen was no longer in a rush or held the same interest as before in refining the tribulation skeleton. In fact, he had been staying at the first layer on the very edge of the Myriad Tribulations Storm.

Previously Zen had successfully refined his Chaotic Source Spirits by the method of "being beaten." The rate at which they grew was astoundingly fast. It didn't take long before Zen made his way to the late stage of the Chaotic Source Realm.

When he attempted to refine the Chaotic Source Spirits with the assistance of the blue-golden water drops in the Myriad Tribulation Storm, he was also "being beaten." But this method proved to be more effective.

The tiny light dots that signified the Chaotic Source Spirits were going through the constant process of being rinsed and refined. They were as minuscule as a needle tip in size. Over and over, they extinguished and lit up, then extinguished and lit up in an endless loop. While this method kept on repeating itself, the tiny particles of light simultaneously grew.

This sensation felt quite subtle. It resembled the feeling of countless seeds spreading and breaking through their roots inside his body, and slowly branching their way out. It was as if the Truth of Godly Way acted as an enzyme and sped up the process by infusing itself with them.

In just half a day, the size of the light spots had more than doubled.

Not only did they grow in size each passing minute, but their endurance to the power rose to a higher degree as well. With his newly acquired strength and resistance, Zen effortlessly took a step forward and made his way onto the second layer.

With this action of his, he attracted various curious eyes towards him that belonged to the creatures on the Other Shore.

After Zen's month-long stay on the sixteenth layer, it could be said that the first and second layers didn't prove fruitful enough for him, which was most of the reason why the Other Shore creatures failed to conclude his motives.

Of course, Zen didn't explain to them either. Instead, he chose to prioritize his refinement and kept all his focus on it alone. Slowly and gradually, as he moved forward, the light dots kept on growing in unison with his steps.

When the light dots grew to a certain degree, Zen began to count them carefully. They appeared to have tripled in numbers as the once two hundred Chaotic Source Spirits had now increased to six hundred.

"To conclude everything I know, the two hundred Chaotic Source Spirits can absorb about ten thousand divine megatons of force. When I cultivate to the late stage of the Chaotic Source Realm once more, I can resist the attack of more than thirty thousand divine megatons of force only by the help of Chaotic Source Spirits."

Watching the Chaotic Source Spirits' rapid growth, Zen couldn't help but feel his heart flutter with joy.

He had entered the Land of Bone Tribulation intending to cultivate a Myriad Tribulations Body. The sudden surprise of the growth of Chaotic Source Spirits came as an unexpected gain for him, so he couldn't help but feel giddy over his recent discovery.

With only fifty hours remaining, Zen moved to the third layer. Meanwhile, the tiny light dots-like Chaotic Source Spirits slowly grew till each of them manifested itself into the size of an ant from its previous form of a needle tip.

When the time limit expired, the Myriad Tribulations Storm slowly subsided.

Just as the storm began to soothe up, the blue Soul Interdicting Water and the golden liquid retreated, respectively. As these events unfolded, a swarm of monsters swam their way out of the surrounding walls formed by the Soul Interdicting Water.

In addition to the Ghost-claw Worms, there were also various other unknown creatures. They had varying appearances, and their figures differed from one another. Their unknown origins made them a bigger threat as they glanced the Other Shore creatures in the inner space with eyes brimming with malice.

"The Myriad Tribulations Storm has stopped. Move quickly and get out of here!"

"The seawater will gather up soon enough. If we fall into the sea, we will be doomed..."

"Let's head up..."

Since the surrounding seawater slowly squeezed itself to pave its way towards the center, the space would soon be filled, leaving them nowhere to go.

Similar to the rules at Soul City, outsiders were not allowed to stay after the Land of Bone Tribulation was closed.

Taking caution to the situation, Zen lightly tapped on the bone plate with his tiptoe and flew up towards the bone stairs.

As for the tribulation skeletons, they remained on the bone plates and were eventually flooded by the Soul Interdicting Water.

Once Zen and the Other Shore creatures pushed their way out of the huge head, the jaws made clicking sound again. As if triggering something, the mouth closed up, and the head began to descend. The only thing it left to vouch for its existence was the skull that was left outside.

After a good round of rinsing and refining, the Other Shore creatures felt their enmity towards Zen dissolve. Some of them even revealed hints of high respect and goodwill towards him on their faces.

However, they were increasingly curious about the kind of body refining technique Zen had used.

Of course, Zen didn't let them in on any of the details. Besides, it would have been useless even if he decided to tell them.

The Chaotic Source Spirits on the Other Shore existed in a different form from those in the Source World.

The Chaotic Source Spirits from the Other Shore were ordinary creatures who harbored average strength. Even if they were carried by someone from the Source World as an Other Shore Token of the auxiliary type, their abilities would display minimal improvements.

However, in the Source World, the reproduced Chaotic Source Spirits took the form of life between the Other Shore and the Source World. They did not stray from the truth, and they could stay in the Source World.

The crystals found inside the bodies of the Chaotic Source Spirits held the ability to absorb energy and resist against damage. These Other Shore creatures were unable to see the crystals lying dormant in the bodies of the Chaotic Source Spirits, and they didn't carry anything.

The creatures from the Other Shore couldn't leave the Other Shore. For the next eight hundred hours, they were left with no choice but to wait it out and stay on the bone island.

The member of the Sturdy Bull race wasted no time and proceeded to draw himself a peculiar array on the ground. Once it was complete, he stepped inside and sat down to concentrate on cultivating his body refining method.

On the other hand, the centipede found himself a hollow bone and curled up inside it to rest his eyes and sleep. His protection theurgy seemed to have drained a considerable amount of his energy. He lay there and rested to recuperate after his month-long stay in the Myriad Tribulations Storm.

Zen bid his time and waited for the effect of the Soul Interdicting Water to wear off. Then, he left the Other Shore to learn about the current situation in the Source World.

The past month, the Source World had undergone a few mishaps that threatened its peace, but nothing too serious. However, it seemed Libby was encountering a few issues which prevented her from going to Stage ThirtyTwo of the Other Shore.

According to her, the bones in the Sanskrit Light Stage that led to the top seemed to have been destroyed, and this kind of damage probably had something to do with the changes in the Sanskrit Light Stage.

Having no other choice, she had to reluctantly retreat to the largest bone cavity. After this, she chose to leave the Other Shore for a short period.

Libby had no one she could trust in the Sanskrit Light Stage. Helpless as she was, all she could do was wait. Maybe if Zen were to pass through the Land of Bone Tribulation, she could turn the tables in her favor? Meanwhile, Elizabeth had gained a firm foothold and strengthened her position in Stage Thirty of the Other Shore.

Elizabeth had plans to summon her powerful clansmen of the Holy Soul Realm, from Stage Thirty-two of the Other Shore. She had debriefed the news to the Oneness Sky Palace. Pearce and the others felt themselves well up with joy upon hearing this from her. Stage Thirty of the Other Shore held significance in terms of its location. If humans were to gain control of this stage, the benefits would be incalculable.

The Holy Souls residing in Stage Thirty-two were refused access to go down. Even so, the Holy Souls currently in Stage Twenty-nine and Twentyeight of the Other Shore were able to move up to get there. Although the Holy Souls combined from both stages weren't dominant in numbers, they were enough to lend Elizabeth a hand.

During this period, the Element Spirit race had also dispatched FiveElement Slaves from the higher stage. Unfortunately for them, they were quickly obliterated by Pompeo, the bald giant.

The Other Shore creatures residing in Stage Thirty had no other choice but to pick the easier option and surrender, or they would have been asked to leave.
